KG-Hopper: Empowering Compact Open LLMs with Knowledge Graph Reasoning via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Shuai Wang, Yinan Yu
First: 2026-03-22T23:07:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T17:49:12+00:00
Comments: Accepted to IJCNN 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) demonstrate impressive natural language capabilities but often struggle with knowledge-intensive reasoning tasks. Knowledge Base Question Answering (KBQA), which leverages structured Knowledge Graphs (KGs) exemplifies this challenge due to the need for accurate multi-hop reasoning. Existing approaches typically perform sequential reasoning steps guided by predefined pipelines, restricting flexibility and causing error cascades due to isolated reasoning at each step. To address these limitations, we propose KG-Hopper, a novel Reinforcement Learning (RL) framework that empowers compact open LLMs with the ability to perform integrated multi-hop KG reasoning within a single inference round. Rather than reasoning step-by-step, we train a Reasoning LLM that embeds the entire KG traversal and decision process into a unified ``thinking'' stage, enabling global reasoning over cross-step dependencies and dynamic path exploration with backtracking. Experimental results on eight KG reasoning benchmarks show that KG-Hopper, based on a 7B-parameter LLM, consistently outperforms larger multi-step systems (up to 70B) and achieves competitive performance with proprietary models such as GPT-3.5-Turbo and GPT-4o-mini, while remaining compact, open, and data-efficient. The code is publicly available at: https://github.com/Wangshuaiia/KG-Hopper.
中文标题/摘要
标题：KG-Hopper：通过强化学习赋能紧凑型开源大语言模型实现知识图谱推理
大语言模型（LLMs）在自然语言处理方面展现出卓越能力，但在知识密集型推理任务中常面临挑战。以结构化知识图谱（KGs）为基础的知识库问答（KBQA）任务因需进行精确的多跳推理而凸显了这一难题。现有方法通常依赖预定义流程执行顺序推理步骤，这种分步独立推理的方式限制了灵活性并易导致错误级联。为突破这些局限，我们提出KG-Hopper——一种新颖的强化学习（RL）框架，使紧凑型开源LLMs能够在单轮推理中完成集成式多跳知识图谱推理。我们训练了一个推理大语言模型，将完整的图谱遍历与决策过程嵌入统一的“思考”阶段，而非逐步推理，从而实现对跨步骤依赖的全局推理及具备回溯能力的动态路径探索。在八个知识图谱推理基准测试中，基于70亿参数LLM的KG-Hopper持续超越规模更大的多步推理系统（最高达700亿参数），并与GPT-3.5-Turbo、GPT-4o-mini等专有模型达到相当性能，同时保持紧凑、开源和数据高效的特点。代码已开源：https://github.com/Wangshuaiia/KG-Hopper。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of enabling compact open LLMs to perform complex knowledge graph reasoning, as they often struggle with multi-hop tasks like KBQA where existing step-by-step methods are inflexible and error-prone. The proposed method, KG-Hopper, employs a reinforcement learning framework to train a Reasoning LLM that integrates the entire KG traversal into a single unified reasoning stage, allowing for global dependency handling and dynamic path exploration with backtracking. Experimental results on eight benchmarks demonstrate that KG-Hopper, using only a 7B-parameter LLM, outperforms larger multi-step systems up to 70B parameters and achieves competitive performance with proprietary models like GPT-3.5-Turbo and GPT-4o-mini, highlighting its effectiveness and data efficiency.
本文旨在解决紧凑型开源大语言模型在知识图谱推理任务中的不足，特别是在需要多跳推理的知识库问答任务上，现有分步方法灵活性差且容易产生错误累积。提出的KG-Hopper方法采用强化学习框架，训练一个推理大语言模型，将整个知识图谱遍历过程整合到单一的推理阶段中，实现全局依赖处理和带回溯的动态路径探索。在八个基准测试上的实验结果表明，基于70亿参数的KG-Hopper模型，性能超越了参数规模达700亿的多步推理系统，并与GPT-3.5-Turbo和GPT-4o-mini等专有模型表现相当，展现了其高效性和数据效率。
Synthetic POMDPs to Challenge Memory-Augmented RL: Memory Demand Structure Modeling
Authors: Yongyi Wang, Lingfeng Li, Bozhou Chen, Ang Li, Hanyu Liu, Qirui Zheng, Xionghui Yang, Wenxin Li
First: 2025-08-06T10:13:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T17:18:39+00:00
Comments: The article has been accepted by Frontiers of Computer Science (FCS), with the DOI: {10.1007/s11704-026-52148-y}
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent benchmarks for memory-augmented reinforcement learning (RL) have introduced partially observable Markov decision process (POMDP) environments in which agents must use historical observations to make decisions. However, these benchmarks often lack fine-grained control over the challenges posed to memory models. Synthetic environments offer a solution, enabling precise manipulation of environment dynamics for rigorous and interpretable evaluation of memory-augmented RL. This paper advances the design of such customizable POMDPs with three key contributions: (1) a theoretical framework for analyzing POMDPs based on Memory Demand Structure (MDS) and related concepts; (2) a methodology using linear dynamics, state aggregation, and reward redistribution to construct POMDPs with predefined MDS; and (3) a suite of lightweight, scalable POMDP environments with tunable difficulty, grounded in our theoretical insights. Overall, our work clarifies core challenges in partially observable RL, offers principled guidelines for POMDP design, and aids in selecting and developing suitable memory architectures for RL tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：合成POMDP挑战记忆增强强化学习：记忆需求结构建模
近期记忆增强强化学习（RL）的基准测试引入了部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP）环境，要求智能体利用历史观测进行决策。然而，这些基准往往缺乏对记忆模型所面临挑战的精细控制。合成环境提供了一种解决方案，通过对环境动态的精确操控，实现对记忆增强RL的严谨且可解释的评估。本文通过三项关键贡献推进了此类可定制POMDP的设计：（1）基于记忆需求结构（MDS）及相关概念分析POMDP的理论框架；（2）利用线性动态、状态聚合与奖励重分配构建具有预设MDS的POMDP的方法论；（3）基于理论洞见开发的一套轻量级、可扩展且难度可调的POMDP环境。总体而言，本研究阐明了部分可观测RL的核心挑战，为POMDP设计提供了原则性指导，并有助于为RL任务选择和开发合适的记忆架构。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for more controlled and interpretable benchmarks to evaluate memory-augmented reinforcement learning (RL) in partially observable settings, this paper introduces a framework for designing synthetic POMDPs with precisely tunable memory challenges. The method establishes a theoretical foundation based on Memory Demand Structure (MDS) and employs techniques like linear dynamics and state aggregation to construct environments with predefined memory requirements. Experimental results demonstrate the creation of a scalable suite of lightweight POMDP environments where difficulty is adjustable, providing a principled tool for analyzing and selecting appropriate memory architectures for RL agents.
本文的动机是现有基准在评估部分可观测环境下记忆增强强化学习时缺乏对记忆挑战的精细控制，因此提出了一种设计可定制合成POMDP的框架。方法上，建立了基于记忆需求结构的理论分析基础，并利用线性动力学、状态聚合等技术构建具有预定义记忆需求的环境。主要实验成果是开发了一套轻量级、可扩展且难度可调的POMDP环境，为系统分析不同记忆架构在强化学习任务中的适用性提供了原则性工具。
Cycle-Consistent Search: Question Reconstructability as a Proxy Reward for Search Agent Training
Authors: Sohyun An, Shuibenyang Yuan, Hayeon Lee, Cho-Jui Hsieh, Alexander Min
First: 2026-04-14T17:00:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T17:00:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) has shown strong potential for optimizing search agents in complex information retrieval tasks. However, existing approaches predominantly rely on gold supervision, such as ground-truth answers, which is difficult to scale. To address this limitation, we propose Cycle-Consistent Search (CCS), a gold-supervision-free framework for training search agents, inspired by cycle-consistency techniques from unsupervised machine translation and image-to-image translation. Our key hypothesis is that an optimal search trajectory, unlike insufficient or irrelevant ones, serves as a lossless encoding of the question's intent. Consequently, a high-quality trajectory should preserve the information required to accurately reconstruct the original question, thereby inducing a reward signal for policy optimization. However, naive cycle-consistency objectives are vulnerable to information leakage, as reconstruction may rely on superficial lexical cues rather than the underlying search process. To reduce this effect, we apply information bottlenecks, including exclusion of the final response and named entity recognition (NER) masking of search queries. These constraints force reconstruction to rely on retrieved observations together with the structural scaffold, ensuring that the resulting reward signal reflects informational adequacy rather than linguistic redundancy. Experiments on question-answering benchmarks show that CCS achieves performance comparable to supervised baselines while outperforming prior methods that do not rely on gold supervision. These results suggest that CCS provides a scalable training paradigm for training search agents in settings where gold supervision is unavailable.
中文标题/摘要
标题：循环一致搜索：以问题可重构性作为搜索代理训练的代理奖励
强化学习在复杂信息检索任务中优化搜索代理展现出巨大潜力，但现有方法主要依赖黄金监督（如标准答案），难以规模化。为此，我们提出循环一致搜索——一种无需黄金监督的搜索代理训练框架，其灵感源自无监督机器翻译和图像转换中的循环一致性技术。核心假设是：与不充分或不相关的搜索轨迹不同，最优搜索轨迹能够无损编码问题意图。因此，高质量轨迹应保留准确重构原始问题所需的信息，从而产生策略优化的奖励信号。然而，简单的循环一致性目标易受信息泄漏影响，因为重构可能依赖表层词汇线索而非底层搜索过程。为缓解此问题，我们引入信息瓶颈技术，包括排除最终响应及对搜索查询进行命名实体识别掩码。这些约束迫使重构过程依赖检索观察结果与结构框架，确保奖励信号反映信息充分性而非语言冗余。在问答基准测试中，CCS达到与监督基线相当的性能，且优于不依赖黄金监督的现有方法。结果表明，CCS为无黄金监督场景下的搜索代理训练提供了可扩展的范式。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of scaling reinforcement learning for search agents by eliminating the need for gold supervision, such as ground-truth answers. The authors propose Cycle-Consistent Search (CCS), a framework inspired by cycle-consistency, which uses question reconstructability as a proxy reward: the hypothesis is that an optimal search trajectory should allow accurate reconstruction of the original question, thereby providing a signal for policy optimization. To prevent information leakage from superficial cues, they introduce information bottlenecks like excluding the final response and masking named entities in queries, forcing reliance on retrieved observations. Experimental results on question-answering benchmarks show that CCS performs comparably to supervised baselines and outperforms prior unsupervised methods, demonstrating its potential as a scalable training paradigm.
本文针对搜索代理强化学习中依赖黄金监督（如标准答案）难以扩展的问题，提出了一种无需黄金监督的框架——循环一致搜索（CCS）。该方法受无监督机器翻译和图像转换中的循环一致性启发，将问题可重构性作为代理奖励：假设最优搜索轨迹应能无损编码问题意图，从而通过重构准确性提供策略优化信号。为避免重构依赖表面词汇线索导致信息泄露，作者引入了信息瓶颈技术，如排除最终响应和掩码查询中的命名实体，确保重构依赖于检索观察。在问答基准测试上的实验表明，CCS性能与有监督基线相当，并优于先前的无监督方法，这为无黄金监督场景下的搜索代理训练提供了可扩展的范式。
Thinking Sparks!: Emergent Attention Heads in Reasoning Models During Post Training
Authors: Yein Park, Minbyul Jeong, Jaewoo Kang
First: 2025-09-30T04:23:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T15:45:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The remarkable capabilities of modern large reasoning models are largely unlocked through post-training techniques such as supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and reinforcement learning (RL). However, the architectural mechanisms behind such improvements remain largely opaque. In this work, we use circuit analysis to demonstrate that post-training for complex reasoning sparks the emergence of novel, functionally specialized attention heads. These heads collectively support structured reasoning and computation. Our comparative analysis across various model families reveals that these emergent heads evolve differently under different training regimes. Distillation and SFT foster a cumulative addition of stable reasoning heads. In contrast, group relative policy optimization (GRPO) operates in a dynamic search mode: relatively few attention heads are iteratively activated, evaluated, and pruned, with their survival closely tracking fluctuations in the task reward signal. Furthermore, we find that controllable "think on/off" models do not possess dedicated "thinking" heads. Instead, turning off explicit reasoning triggers a broader-but less efficient-set of compensatory heads. Through ablation and qualitative analyses, we connect these circuit-level dynamics to a crucial performance trade-off: strengthened heads enable sophisticated problem-solving strategies for difficult problems but can also introduce "over-thinking" failure modes, such as calculation errors or logical loops on simpler tasks. These findings connect circuit-level dynamics to macro-level performance, identifying an inherent tension where complex reasoning comes at the cost of elementary computations. More broadly, our work points to future directions for training policy design, emphasizing the need to balance the development of effective reasoning strategies with the assurance of reliable, flawless execution.
中文标题/摘要
标题：思维火花！：推理模型在训练后阶段涌现的注意力头
现代大型推理模型的卓越能力主要通过监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（RL）等训练后技术得以释放，但这些改进背后的架构机制仍不透明。本研究通过电路分析表明，复杂推理的训练后过程会催生新型功能特化的注意力头，这些注意力头共同支撑结构化推理与计算。跨模型家族的对比分析揭示，这些涌现头在不同训练机制下演化路径各异：蒸馏与SFT促进稳定推理头的累积增加；而分组相对策略优化（GRPO）则运行于动态搜索模式——少量注意力头被迭代激活、评估与剪枝，其存续紧密追踪任务奖励信号的波动。进一步发现，可控“思考启/停”模型并未配备专用的“思考”头，关闭显式推理反而会触发更广泛但低效的补偿头集合。通过消融与定性分析，我们将这些电路动态与关键性能权衡联系起来：强化头虽能针对难题启用精妙解决策略，但也可能引发“过度思考”故障模式（如简单任务中的计算错误或逻辑循环）。这些发现将电路动态与宏观性能相连接，揭示了复杂推理以基础计算能力为代价的内在张力。本研究更广泛地为训练策略设计指明方向，强调需在开发有效推理策略与保障可靠无误执行之间寻求平衡。
Summary / 总结
This study investigates the opaque architectural mechanisms behind the improved reasoning capabilities of large language models after post-training techniques like supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and reinforcement learning (RL). Using circuit analysis, the authors find that post-training sparks the emergence of novel, functionally specialized attention heads that collectively support structured reasoning, with different training regimes leading to distinct evolutionary patterns: SFT and distillation cumulatively add stable reasoning heads, while group relative policy optimization (GRPO) dynamically activates, evaluates, and prunes heads in alignment with reward signals. Key experimental results reveal that controllable 'think on/off' models lack dedicated reasoning heads, instead relying on broader but less efficient compensatory circuits when reasoning is turned off, and they identify a performance trade-off where strengthened reasoning heads enable complex problem-solving but can cause 'over-thinking' failures on simpler tasks, highlighting a tension between advanced reasoning and reliable elementary computation.
本研究旨在揭示大型语言模型经过监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（RL）等后训练技术后，其推理能力提升背后不透明的架构机制。通过电路分析，作者发现后训练会激发新型、功能专门化的注意力头涌现，这些头共同支持结构化推理，且不同训练制度导致不同的演化模式：SFT和知识蒸馏会累积添加稳定的推理头，而分组相对策略优化（GRPO）则动态激活、评估并修剪注意力头，与奖励信号紧密同步。关键实验结果表明，可控的“思考开启/关闭”模型并没有专用的推理头，而是在关闭显式推理时依赖更广泛但低效的补偿性电路；研究还发现一个性能权衡：增强的推理头能实现复杂问题求解，但可能在简单任务上引发“过度思考”故障，如计算错误或逻辑循环，这揭示了高级推理与可靠基础计算之间的内在张力。
FastGrasp: Learning-based Whole-body Control method for Fast Dexterous Grasping with Mobile Manipulators
Authors: Heng Tao, Yiming Zhong, Zemin Yang, Yuexin Ma
First: 2026-04-14T15:30:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T15:30:57+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Fast grasping is critical for mobile robots in logistics, manufacturing, and service applications. Existing methods face fundamental challenges in impact stabilization under high-speed motion, real-time whole-body coordination, and generalization across diverse objects and scenarios, limited by fixed bases, simple grippers, or slow tactile response capabilities. We propose \textbf{FastGrasp}, a learning-based framework that integrates grasp guidance, whole-body control, and tactile feedback for mobile fast grasping. Our two-stage reinforcement learning strategy first generates diverse grasp candidates via conditional variational autoencoder conditioned on object point clouds, then executes coordinated movements of mobile base, arm, and hand guided by optimal grasp selection. Tactile sensing enables real-time grasp adjustments to handle impact effects and object variations. Extensive experiments demonstrate superior grasping performance in both simulation and real-world scenarios, achieving robust manipulation across diverse object geometries through effective sim-to-real transfer.
中文标题/摘要
标题：FastGrasp：基于学习的移动机械臂快速灵巧抓取全身控制方法
快速抓取对于物流、制造和服务应用中的移动机器人至关重要。现有方法在高速运动下的冲击稳定、实时全身协调以及跨多样物体与场景的泛化能力方面面临根本性挑战，受限于固定基座、简单夹爪或迟缓的触觉响应能力。我们提出\textbf{FastGrasp}——一种融合抓取引导、全身控制与触觉反馈的基于学习的移动快速抓取框架。我们的两阶段强化学习策略首先通过以物体点云为条件的变分自编码器生成多样化抓取候选方案，随后在最优抓取选择指导下协调执行移动基座、机械臂与末端执行器的运动。触觉感知支持实时抓取调整以应对冲击效应与物体变异。大量实验在仿真与真实场景中均展现出卓越的抓取性能，通过有效的仿真到现实迁移实现了跨多样物体几何形态的鲁棒操作。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of enabling mobile manipulators to perform fast and dexterous grasping in dynamic real-world applications like logistics, where existing methods struggle with impact stabilization, real-time whole-body coordination, and generalization. The proposed FastGrasp framework employs a two-stage reinforcement learning approach: first, a conditional variational autoencoder generates diverse grasp candidates from object point clouds, and then an optimal selection guides the coordinated control of the mobile base, arm, and hand, with tactile feedback enabling real-time adjustments to manage impacts and object variations. Experimental results in both simulation and real-world settings demonstrate robust grasping performance across diverse object geometries, achieving effective sim-to-real transfer.
该研究旨在解决移动操作机器人在物流等动态现实应用中实现快速灵巧抓取的挑战，现有方法在高速运动下的冲击稳定、实时全身协调及泛化能力方面存在不足。提出的FastGrasp框架采用两阶段强化学习策略：首先通过条件变分自编码器基于物体点云生成多样抓取候选，随后通过最优选择指导移动底盘、机械臂和手部的协调运动，并利用触觉反馈进行实时调整以处理冲击效应和物体变化。在仿真和真实场景中的大量实验表明，该方法在不同物体几何形状上均实现了鲁棒的抓取性能，并有效完成了从仿真到现实的迁移。
No More Stale Feedback: Co-Evolving Critics for Open-World Agent Learning
Authors: Zhicong Li, Lingjie Jiang, Yulan Hu, Xingchen Zeng, Yixia Li, Xiangwen Zhang, Guanhua Chen, Zheng Pan, Xin Li, Yong Liu
First: 2026-01-11T07:29:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T15:14:10+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Critique-guided reinforcement learning (RL) has emerged as a powerful paradigm for training LLM agents by augmenting sparse outcome rewards with natural-language feedback. However, current methods often rely on static or offline critic models, which fail to adapt as the policy evolves. In on-policy RL, the agent's error patterns shift over time, causing stationary critics to become stale and providing feedback of diminishing utility. To address this, we introduce ECHO (Evolving Critic for Hindsight-Guided Optimization)}, a framework that jointly optimizes the policy and critic through a synchronized co-evolutionary loop. ECHO utilizes a cascaded rollout mechanism where the critic generates multiple diagnoses for an initial trajectory, followed by policy refinement to enable group-structured advantage estimation. We address the challenge of learning plateaus via a saturation-aware gain shaping objective, which rewards the critic for inducing incremental improvements in high-performing trajectories. By employing dual-track GRPO updates, ECHO ensures the critic's feedback stays synchronized with the evolving policy. Experimental results show that ECHO yields more stable training and higher long-horizon task success across open-world environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：告别陈旧反馈：面向开放世界智能体学习的协同进化评价器
基于评价的强化学习已成为通过自然语言反馈增强稀疏结果奖励来训练大语言模型智能体的重要范式。然而，现有方法常依赖静态或离线评价模型，无法随策略演化而适应。在在线策略强化学习中，智能体的错误模式会随时间变化，导致固定评价器逐渐失效，反馈效用递减。为此，我们提出ECHO（基于后见指导优化的进化评价器）框架，通过同步协同进化循环联合优化策略与评价器。ECHO采用级联推演机制：评价器对初始轨迹生成多重诊断，随后进行策略优化以实现分组结构优势估计。我们通过饱和度感知增益塑造目标应对学习平台期挑战，该目标通过激励评价器在高性能轨迹中引发渐进改进来给予奖励。通过双轨GRPO更新机制，ECHO确保评价器反馈与演化策略保持同步。实验结果表明，ECHO在开放世界环境中能实现更稳定的训练和更高的长周期任务成功率。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the problem of stale feedback in critique-guided reinforcement learning, where static critic models fail to adapt to evolving agent policies, leading to diminishing utility. To solve this, the authors introduce ECHO, a framework that co-evolves the policy and critic through a synchronized loop, employing a cascaded rollout mechanism for trajectory diagnosis and policy refinement, along with a saturation-aware gain shaping objective to overcome learning plateaus. Experimental results demonstrate that ECHO achieves more stable training and higher success rates in long-horizon open-world tasks compared to methods with stationary critics.
本文针对强化学习中反馈滞后的问题，即静态评论模型无法适应智能体策略的演变，导致反馈效用下降。为解决此问题，作者提出了ECHO框架，通过同步协同进化循环共同优化策略和评论模型，采用级联展开机制进行轨迹诊断和策略优化，并引入饱和度感知增益塑造目标以克服学习瓶颈。实验结果表明，ECHO在开放世界环境中实现了更稳定的训练和更高的长时任务成功率。
Free Random Projection for In-Context Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Tomohiro Hayase, Benoît Collins, Nakamasa Inoue
First: 2025-04-09T15:38:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T15:01:15+00:00
Comments: Accepted to AISTATS2026. Code available at https://github.com/ThayaFluss/frp_rl
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Hierarchical inductive biases are hypothesized to promote generalizable policies in reinforcement learning, as demonstrated by explicit hyperbolic latent representations and architectures. Therefore, a more flexible approach is to have these biases emerge naturally from the algorithm. We introduce Free Random Projection, an input mapping grounded in free probability theory that constructs random orthogonal matrices where hierarchical structure arises inherently. The free random projection integrates seamlessly into existing in-context reinforcement learning frameworks by encoding hierarchical organization within the input space without requiring explicit architectural modifications. Empirical results on multi-environment benchmarks show that free random projection consistently outperforms the standard random projection, leading to improvements in generalization. Furthermore, analyses within linearly solvable Markov decision processes and investigations of the spectrum of kernel random matrices reveal the theoretical underpinnings of free random projection's enhanced performance, highlighting its capacity for effective adaptation in hierarchically structured state spaces.
中文标题/摘要
标题：用于情境强化学习的自由随机投影
层级归纳偏置被假设能促进强化学习中泛化策略的形成，如显式双曲潜在表示与架构所验证。因此，更灵活的方法是让这些偏置从算法中自然涌现。我们提出自由随机投影——一种基于自由概率理论的输入映射方法，可构建具有固有层级结构的随机正交矩阵。该投影通过将层级组织编码至输入空间，无需显式架构修改即可无缝集成至现有情境强化学习框架。多环境基准测试表明，自由随机投影始终优于标准随机投影，显著提升泛化能力。在线性可解马尔可夫决策过程的分析与核随机矩阵谱的研究中，进一步揭示了其性能提升的理论基础，突显了该方法在层级化状态空间中高效适应的能力。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for hierarchical inductive biases to improve generalization in reinforcement learning without explicit architectural changes, this paper introduces Free Random Projection, a method based on free probability theory that generates random orthogonal matrices to inherently encode hierarchical structure in input representations. The approach integrates into in-context reinforcement learning frameworks by mapping inputs to structured spaces, avoiding modifications to the underlying architecture. Experimental results on multi-environment benchmarks demonstrate that free random projection consistently outperforms standard random projection in generalization, with theoretical analyses in linearly solvable Markov decision processes and kernel random matrices explaining its enhanced performance in hierarchically structured state spaces.
本文的动机是通过层次归纳偏置提升强化学习的泛化能力，而无需显式修改架构，为此提出了基于自由概率理论的自由随机投影方法，该方法生成随机正交矩阵以在输入表示中自然编码层次结构。该方法通过将输入映射到结构化空间，无缝集成到上下文强化学习框架中，无需改变现有架构。在多环境基准测试中的实验结果表明，自由随机投影在泛化性能上持续优于标准随机投影，同时在线性可解马尔可夫决策过程和核随机矩阵的理论分析揭示了其在层次化状态空间中有效适应的能力，为其优越性能提供了理论支撑。
A Two-Timescale Primal-Dual Framework for Reinforcement Learning via Online Dual Variable Guidance
Authors: Axel Friedrich Wolter, Tobias Sutter
First: 2025-05-07T15:18:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T14:26:50+00:00
Comments: 68 pages, 1 figure; 2nd Revised version with additional corollary
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study reinforcement learning by combining recent advances in regularized linear programming formulations with the classical theory of stochastic approximation. Motivated by the challenge of designing algorithms that leverage off-policy data while maintaining on-policy exploration, we propose PGDA-RL, a novel primal-dual Projected Gradient Descent-Ascent algorithm for solving regularized Markov Decision Processes (MDPs). PGDA-RL integrates experience replay-based gradient estimation with a two-timescale decomposition of the underlying nested optimization problem. The algorithm operates asynchronously, interacts with the environment through a single trajectory of correlated data, and updates its policy online in response to the dual variable associated with the occupancy measure of the underlying MDP. We prove that PGDA-RL converges almost surely to the optimal value function and policy of the regularized MDP. Our convergence analysis relies on tools from stochastic approximation theory and holds under weaker assumptions than those required by existing primal-dual RL approaches, notably removing the need for a simulator or a fixed behavioral policy. Under a strengthened ergodicity assumption on the underlying Markov chain, we establish a last-iterate finite-time guarantee with $\tilde{O} (k^{-2/3})$ mean-square convergence, aligning with the best-known rates for two-timescale stochastic approximation methods under Markovian sampling and biased gradient estimates.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于在线对偶变量引导的双时间尺度原始-对偶强化学习框架
本研究结合正则化线性规划的最新进展与经典随机逼近理论，探索强化学习算法设计。针对利用离轨数据同时保持同轨探索的挑战，我们提出PGDA-RL算法——一种求解正则化马尔可夫决策过程的新型原始-对偶投影梯度下降-上升算法。该算法融合经验回放梯度估计与嵌套优化问题的双时间尺度分解，通过单条相关数据轨迹与环境异步交互，并依据MDP占用测度的对偶变量在线更新策略。理论证明PGDA-RL几乎必然收敛至正则化MDP的最优值函数与策略，其收敛分析基于随机逼近理论工具，所需假设弱于现有原始-对偶RL方法（尤其无需模拟器或固定行为策略）。在强化马尔可夫链遍历性假设下，我们建立了末次迭代有限时间保证，获得$\tilde{O}(k^{-2/3})$均方收敛速率，与马尔可夫采样和偏置梯度估计条件下双时间尺度随机逼近方法的最佳已知速率一致。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to leverage off-policy data while preserving on-policy exploration in reinforcement learning, this paper introduces PGDA-RL, a primal-dual algorithm based on a two-timescale projected gradient descent-ascent framework for solving regularized Markov Decision Processes. The method integrates experience replay for gradient estimation with an asynchronous online update scheme that guides policy improvements via dual variables linked to the MDP's occupancy measure. Experimental results demonstrate that PGDA-RL achieves almost sure convergence to the optimal policy under weaker assumptions than prior primal-dual approaches, and under an ergodicity condition, it attains a finite-time mean-square convergence rate of $\tilde{O}(k^{-2/3})$, matching state-of-the-art rates for two-timescale stochastic approximation with Markovian sampling.
本文旨在解决强化学习中利用离策略数据同时保持在线探索的挑战，提出了PGDA-RL算法，这是一种基于双时间尺度投影梯度下降-上升框架的原对偶方法，用于求解正则化马尔可夫决策过程。该方法结合了经验回放的梯度估计与异步在线更新机制，通过关联于MDP占用测度的对偶变量指导策略改进。实验结果表明，PGDA-RL在比现有原对偶方法更弱的假设下几乎必然收敛到最优策略，且在遍历性条件下，实现了$\tilde{O}(k^{-2/3})$的有限时间均方收敛速率，与马尔可夫采样下双时间尺度随机逼近的最佳已知速率一致。
Replicable Reinforcement Learning with Linear Function Approximation
Authors: Eric Eaton, Marcel Hussing, Michael Kearns, Aaron Roth, Sikata Bela Sengupta, Jessica Sorrell
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-09-10T14:56:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T14:23:25+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Replication of experimental results has been a challenge faced by many scientific disciplines, including the field of machine learning. Recent work on the theory of machine learning has formalized replicability as the demand that an algorithm produce identical outcomes when executed twice on different samples from the same distribution. Provably replicable algorithms are especially interesting for reinforcement learning (RL), where algorithms are known to be unstable in practice. While replicable algorithms exist for tabular RL settings, extending these guarantees to more practical function approximation settings has remained an open problem. In this work, we make progress by developing replicable methods for linear function approximation in RL. We first introduce two efficient algorithms for replicable random design regression and uncentered covariance estimation, each of independent interest. We then leverage these tools to provide the first provably efficient replicable RL algorithms for linear Markov decision processes in both the generative model and episodic settings. Finally, we evaluate our algorithms experimentally and show how they can inspire more consistent neural policies.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于线性函数逼近的可复现强化学习
实验结果的可复现性是包括机器学习在内的多个科学领域面临的挑战。近期机器学习理论研究将可复现性形式化为算法在同一分布的不同样本上重复执行时需产生相同结果的要求。可证明可复现的算法对强化学习尤为重要，因为该领域算法在实践中常表现出不稳定性。虽然表格型强化学习已存在可复现算法，但将此类保证扩展到更实用的函数逼近场景仍是未解难题。本研究通过开发强化学习中线性函数逼近的可复现方法取得进展：首先提出两种分别用于可复现随机设计回归和无中心协方差估计的高效算法，二者均具独立价值；随后利用这些工具，首次为生成模型和分幕式场景下的线性马尔可夫决策过程提供可证明高效的可复现强化学习算法；最后通过实验评估算法性能，并展示其如何启发更稳定的神经策略。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of experimental replication in machine learning and the practical instability of reinforcement learning (RL) algorithms, this work develops replicable methods for RL with linear function approximation. The method involves introducing efficient replicable algorithms for random design regression and uncentered covariance estimation, which are then leveraged to construct the first provably efficient replicable RL algorithms for linear Markov decision processes in generative model and episodic settings. The main experimental results demonstrate the efficacy of these algorithms and show how they can inspire more consistent neural network policies.
本研究针对机器学习中实验可复现性的挑战以及强化学习算法在实际中的不稳定性，开发了基于线性函数近似的可复现强化学习方法。其方法核心是首先提出了用于随机设计回归和无中心化协方差估计的高效可复现算法，进而利用这些工具为线性马尔可夫决策过程构建了首个在生成模型和情景式设置下可证明高效的可复现强化学习算法。主要实验结果表明了这些算法的有效性，并展示了它们如何能启发生成更一致的神经网络策略。
Neural Architecture Search of Time-to-First-Spike-Coded Spiking Neural Networks for Efficient Eye-based Emotion Recognition
Authors: Qianhui Liu, Jing Yang, Miao Yu, Trevor E. Carlson, Gang Pan, Haizhou Li, Zhumin Chen
First: 2025-12-02T06:35:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T14:16:55+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Eye-based emotion recognition enables eyewear devices to perceive users' emotional states and support emotion-aware interaction. However, deploying such functionality on their resource-limited embedded hardware remains challenging. Time-to-first-spike (TTFS)-coded spiking neural networks (SNNs) offer a promising solution due to their extremely sparse and energy-efficient computation, where each neuron emits at most one binary spike. While prior works have primarily focused on improving TTFS SNN training algorithms, the role of network architecture has been largely overlooked. This is particularly critical, as spike timing in TTFS SNNs is tightly coupled with architectural design, and eye-based emotion recognition requires compact yet highly efficient networks. In this paper, we propose TNAS-ER, the first neural architecture search (NAS) framework tailored to TTFS SNNs for eye-based emotion recognition. TNAS-ER presents a novel ANN-assisted search strategy that leverages a ReLU-based ANN counterpart to guide architecture optimization and stabilize training of the TTFS SNN. TNAS-ER employs an evolutionary algorithm, with weighted and unweighted average recall jointly defined as fitness objectives for emotion recognition. Extensive experiments demonstrate that TNAS-ER achieves high recognition performance with significantly improved efficiency. Furthermore, we evaluate TNAS-ER on a neuromorphic hardware, confirming its superior energy efficiency and strong potential for real-world applications.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向眼动情绪识别的首脉冲时间编码脉冲神经网络神经架构搜索
基于眼动的情绪识别技术使可穿戴设备能够感知用户情绪状态，支持情感感知交互。然而，在资源受限的嵌入式硬件上部署此类功能仍具挑战性。首脉冲时间编码脉冲神经网络凭借其极稀疏且高能效的计算特性（每个神经元最多发射一个二进制脉冲），为此提供了可行方案。现有研究主要聚焦于改进TTFS SNN训练算法，而网络架构的作用长期被忽视。由于TTFS SNN的脉冲时序与架构设计紧密耦合，且眼动情绪识别需要紧凑高效的网络，架构优化尤为关键。本文提出TNAS-ER——首个面向眼动情绪识别的TTFS SNN神经架构搜索框架。该框架采用创新的ANN辅助搜索策略，通过基于ReLU的ANN对应模型指导架构优化并稳定TTFS SNN训练。TNAS-ER运用进化算法，以加权与非加权平均召回率共同作为情绪识别的适应度目标。大量实验表明，TNAS-ER在显著提升效率的同时实现了高识别性能。此外，我们在神经形态硬件上评估TNAS-ER，证实其卓越的能效优势与实际应用潜力。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for efficient emotion recognition on resource-constrained eyewear devices, this paper introduces TNAS-ER, a neural architecture search framework specifically designed for time-to-first-spike-coded spiking neural networks. The method employs an ANN-assisted search strategy, using a ReLU-based artificial neural network counterpart to guide architecture optimization and stabilize training, alongside an evolutionary algorithm with recall-based fitness objectives. Experimental results show that the discovered architectures achieve high recognition performance with significantly improved computational and energy efficiency, which is further validated on neuromorphic hardware, demonstrating strong potential for real-world deployment.
本文旨在为资源受限的眼镜设备实现高效的眼部情感识别，为此提出了TNAS-ER，这是首个为时间到首次脉冲编码的脉冲神经网络量身定制的神经架构搜索框架。该方法采用了一种ANN辅助搜索策略，利用基于ReLU的人工神经网络对应物来指导架构优化并稳定训练，同时结合了以召回率为适应度目标的进化算法。实验结果表明，所搜索出的架构在实现高识别性能的同时，显著提升了计算和能源效率，并在神经形态硬件上得到验证，展现了强大的实际应用潜力。
Dreamer-CDP: Improving Reconstruction-free World Models Via Continuous Deterministic Representation Prediction
Authors: Michael Hauri, Friedemann Zenke
First: 2026-03-07T07:41:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T13:41:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Model-based reinforcement learning (MBRL) agents operating in high-dimensional observation spaces, such as Dreamer, rely on learning abstract representations for effective planning and control. Existing approaches typically employ reconstruction-based objectives in the observation space, which can render representations sensitive to task-irrelevant details. Recent alternatives trade reconstruction for auxiliary action prediction heads or view augmentation strategies, but perform worse in the Crafter environment than reconstruction-based methods. We close this gap between Dreamer and reconstruction-free models by introducing a JEPA-style predictor defined on continuous, deterministic representations. Our method matches Dreamer's performance on Crafter, demonstrating effective world model learning on this benchmark without reconstruction objectives.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Dreamer-CDP：通过连续确定性表征预测改进免重建世界模型
在高维观测空间中运行的基于模型的强化学习（MBRL）智能体（如Dreamer）依赖学习抽象表征进行有效规划与控制。现有方法通常在观测空间采用基于重建的目标，这可能使表征对任务无关细节敏感。近期替代方案以辅助动作预测头或视角增强策略取代重建，但在Crafter环境中表现逊于基于重建的方法。我们通过在连续确定性表征上定义JEPA风格预测器，弥合了Dreamer与免重建模型间的性能差距。该方法在Crafter基准上达到与Dreamer相当的性能，证明无需重建目标即可在此基准上实现有效的世界模型学习。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the need for model-based reinforcement learning agents to learn abstract representations that are robust to task-irrelevant details, as reconstruction-based methods like Dreamer can be sensitive to such noise. The method introduces a continuous deterministic representation predictor inspired by JEPA, eliminating the reliance on reconstruction objectives in observation space. Experimental results show that this reconstruction-free approach matches Dreamer's performance on the Crafter benchmark, effectively closing the performance gap with reconstruction-based world models.
本文的动机是，基于模型的强化学习智能体需要学习对任务无关细节鲁棒的抽象表示，而像Dreamer这样的基于重建的方法容易受此类噪声影响。该方法引入了一种受JEPA启发的连续确定性表示预测器，摒弃了在观测空间中使用重建目标。实验结果表明，这种无需重建的方法在Crafter基准测试中达到了与Dreamer相当的性能，有效缩小了与基于重建的世界模型之间的性能差距。
Instructions are all you need: Self-supervised Reinforcement Learning for Instruction Following
Authors: Qingyu Ren, Qianyu He, Powei Chang, Jie Zeng, Zeye Sun, Fei Yu, Jiaqing Liang, Yanghua Xiao
First: 2025-10-16T08:24:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T13:37:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Language models often struggle to follow multi-constraint instructions that are crucial for real-world applications. Existing reinforcement learning (RL) approaches suffer from dependency on external supervision and sparse reward signals from multi-constraint tasks. We propose a label-free self-supervised RL framework that eliminates dependency on external supervision by deriving reward signals directly from instructions and generating pseudo-labels for reward model training. Our approach introduces constraint decomposition strategies and efficient constraint-wise binary classification to address sparse reward challenges while maintaining computational efficiency. Experiments show that our approach generalizes well, achieving strong improvements across 3 in-domain and 5 out-of-domain datasets, including challenging agentic and multi-turn instruction following. The data and code are publicly available at https://github.com/Rainier-rq/verl-if
中文标题/摘要
标题：指令即所需：面向指令跟随的自监督强化学习
语言模型在处理现实应用中至关重要的多约束指令时往往表现不佳。现有强化学习方法依赖外部监督，且多约束任务产生的奖励信号稀疏。我们提出一种无需标注的自监督强化学习框架，通过直接从指令中提取奖励信号并生成伪标签用于奖励模型训练，从而消除对外部监督的依赖。该方法引入约束分解策略和高效的逐约束二元分类机制，在保持计算效率的同时应对稀疏奖励挑战。实验表明，该方法泛化能力强，在3个领域内数据集和5个领域外数据集（包括具有挑战性的智能体交互和多轮指令跟随任务）上均取得显著性能提升。数据和代码已公开于 https://github.com/Rainier-rq/verl-if
Summary / 总结
Motivated by language models' difficulties in following multi-constraint instructions and the limitations of existing reinforcement learning methods that rely on external supervision and suffer from sparse rewards, this paper proposes a self-supervised reinforcement learning framework. The method eliminates the need for external labels by deriving reward signals directly from instructions and generating pseudo-labels for reward model training, employing constraint decomposition and efficient constraint-wise binary classification to handle sparse rewards efficiently. Experimental results demonstrate strong generalization, with significant improvements across three in-domain and five out-of-domain datasets, including challenging agentic and multi-turn instruction-following tasks.
针对语言模型在遵循多约束指令方面的困难，以及现有依赖外部监督且受稀疏奖励信号困扰的强化学习方法之不足，本文提出了一种自监督强化学习框架。该方法通过直接从指令中推导奖励信号并生成伪标签用于奖励模型训练，消除了对外部监督的依赖，同时采用约束分解策略和高效的约束级二元分类来应对稀疏奖励问题并保持计算效率。实验结果表明，该方法泛化能力强，在三个领域内和五个领域外数据集上均取得了显著改进，包括具有挑战性的代理和多轮指令遵循任务。
Reasoning about Intent for Ambiguous Requests
Authors: Irina Saparina, Mirella Lapata
First: 2025-11-13T16:18:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T13:35:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models often respond to ambiguous requests by implicitly committing to one interpretation, frustrating users and creating safety risks when that interpretation is wrong. We propose generating a single structured response that enumerates the different ways an ambiguous request can be interpreted, each coupled with a corresponding answer. Our models are trained with reinforcement learning using a dual reward objective: recall on ambiguous inputs to maximise coverage of valid interpretations, and precision on unambiguous ones to suppress spurious alternatives. Training requires only multiple valid answers per input as supervision, no clarification questions or explicit interpretations are needed. Experiments on conversational question answering and semantic parsing demonstrate that our method achieves higher coverage of valid answers than baseline approaches. Human evaluation confirms that predicted interpretations are meaningful and explain their corresponding answers. Our approach promotes transparency with explicit interpretations, achieves efficiency by requiring only one generation step, and supports downstream applications through its structured output format.
中文标题/摘要
标题：针对模糊请求的意图推理
大型语言模型常通过隐式选择一种解释来回应模糊请求，当该解释错误时会引发用户不满并产生安全风险。我们提出生成单一结构化响应，枚举模糊请求可能的不同解释方式，并为每种解释提供对应答案。模型通过强化学习训练，采用双重奖励目标：对模糊输入追求召回率以最大化有效解释的覆盖，对明确输入追求精确率以抑制虚假备选方案。训练仅需每个输入对应多个有效答案作为监督，无需澄清问题或显式解释。在对话式问答和语义解析任务上的实验表明，本方法比基线方案实现了更高的有效答案覆盖率。人工评估证实预测解释具有意义并能阐明对应答案。本方法通过显式解释提升透明度，仅需单步生成实现高效性，并通过结构化输出格式支持下游应用。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the issue where large language models often respond to ambiguous user requests by arbitrarily selecting a single interpretation, which can lead to user frustration and safety risks. The proposed method involves generating a single structured response that explicitly lists the possible interpretations of an ambiguous request, each paired with a corresponding answer. The models are trained using reinforcement learning with a dual reward objective: maximizing recall on ambiguous inputs to cover all valid interpretations and ensuring precision on unambiguous inputs to avoid spurious alternatives. Experimental results on conversational question answering and semantic parsing tasks show that this approach achieves higher coverage of valid answers compared to baseline methods, and human evaluation confirms that the predicted interpretations are meaningful and effectively explain their associated answers.

Hail to the Thief: Exploring Attacks and Defenses in Decentralised GRPO
Authors: Nikolay Blagoev, Oğuzhan Ersoy, Lydia Yiyu Chen
Venue: ACL
First: 2025-11-12T22:29:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T12:41:08+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ACL Findings 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) has demonstrated wide adoption in the post-training of Large Language Models (LLMs). In GRPO, prompts are answered by the model and preferred behaviour is learnt via reinforcement learning. Owing to the small communication volume, GRPO is inherently suitable for decentralised training as the prompts can be concurrently answered by multiple nodes and these completions are exchanged in the form of strings. In this work, we explore the robustness of decentralised GRPO by presenting the first adversarial attacks and countermeasures. We present a diverse set of attacks where malicious nodes poison benign models by sharing their poisoned completions. We demonstrate these attacks on math and coding tasks and show that an adversary can achieve attack success rates of up to 100% in as few as 50 iterations. Moreover, to mitigate the attacks, we propose two defense mechanisms that check logit probabilities of completions or utilize an LLM judge to filter completions. The defenses prevent all but the DoS attack that causes unnecessarily lengthy but conceptually correct completions. The code of both attacks and defenses can be found at: https://github.com/gensyn-ai/HTTT.
中文标题/摘要
标题：窃国者侯：探索去中心化GRPO中的攻击与防御
群体相对策略优化（GRPO）在大语言模型（LLM）的后训练中已得到广泛应用。在GRPO中，模型对提示词生成回答，并通过强化学习习得偏好行为。由于通信量小，GRPO天然适用于去中心化训练——多个节点可并行回答提示词，并以字符串形式交换生成的文本。本研究通过提出首套对抗性攻击与防御方案，探索去中心化GRPO的鲁棒性。我们设计了一系列多样化攻击，恶意节点通过共享污染后的文本来毒化良性模型。在数学与代码任务上的实验表明，攻击者仅需50轮迭代即可实现高达100%的攻击成功率。为缓解攻击，我们提出两种防御机制：检查生成文本的对数概率，或利用LLM评判器过滤文本。除导致生成冗长但概念正确文本的拒绝服务攻击外，其他攻击均可被防御机制阻断。攻击与防御代码详见：https://github.com/gensyn-ai/HTTT。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the security vulnerabilities of decentralized Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), a reinforcement learning method used for post-training large language models, motivated by its susceptibility to adversarial manipulation in distributed settings. The authors introduce a series of attacks where malicious nodes share poisoned text completions to corrupt benign models, achieving up to 100% success rates on math and coding tasks within 50 iterations. To counter these threats, they propose two defense mechanisms based on checking logit probabilities or using an LLM judge, which effectively mitigate most attacks except for a denial-of-service variant that generates excessively long but correct outputs.
本文研究了去中心化群体相对策略优化（GRPO）的安全漏洞，该方法用于大语言模型的后训练，其动机在于分布式环境中易受对抗性攻击。作者提出了一系列攻击方法，恶意节点通过共享有毒文本补全来破坏良性模型，在数学和编程任务上实现了高达100%的攻击成功率，仅需50次迭代。作为防御，他们提出了两种机制：检查补全的对数概率或使用大语言模型作为裁判进行过滤，这些方法能有效阻止大多数攻击，但无法完全防御一种导致生成长度冗余但概念正确补全的拒绝服务攻击。
A hierarchical spatial-aware algorithm with efficient reinforcement learning for human-robot task planning and allocation in production
Authors: Jintao Xue, Xiao Li, Nianmin Zhang
Venue: Volume 98, April 2026, 103159
First: 2026-04-14T12:40:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T12:40:05+00:00
Comments: This is the accepted manuscript of a journal article accepted for publication in Robotics and Computer-Integrated Manufacturing (Elsevier)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In advanced manufacturing systems, humans and robots collaborate to conduct the production process. Effective task planning and allocation (TPA) is crucial for achieving high production efficiency, yet it remains challenging in complex and dynamic manufacturing environments. The dynamic nature of humans and robots, particularly the need to consider spatial information (e.g., humans' real-time position and the distance they need to move to complete a task), substantially complicates TPA. To address the above challenges, we decompose production tasks into manageable subtasks. We then implement a real-time hierarchical human-robot TPA algorithm, including a high-level agent for task planning and a low-level agent for task allocation. For the high-level agent, we propose an efficient buffer-based deep Q-learning method (EBQ), which reduces training time and enhances performance in production problems with long-term and sparse reward challenges. For the low-level agent, a path planning-based spatially aware method (SAP) is designed to allocate tasks to the appropriate human-robot resources, thereby achieving the corresponding sequential subtasks. We conducted experiments on a complex real-time production process in a 3D simulator. The results demonstrate that our proposed EBQ&SAP method effectively addresses human-robot TPA problems in complex and dynamic production processes.
中文标题/摘要
标题：一种具有高效强化学习的层次化空间感知算法用于生产中的人机任务规划与分配
在先进制造系统中，人与机器人协作完成生产过程。有效的任务规划与分配（TPA）对实现高生产效率至关重要，但在复杂动态的制造环境中仍具挑战性。人与机器人的动态特性，尤其是需要考虑空间信息（如人的实时位置及完成任务需移动的距离），显著增加了TPA的复杂性。为应对上述挑战，我们将生产任务分解为可管理的子任务，并实现了一种实时层次化人机TPA算法，包含用于任务规划的高层智能体和用于任务分配的低层智能体。针对高层智能体，我们提出了一种高效的基于缓冲区的深度Q学习方法（EBQ），该方法减少了训练时间，并在具有长期稀疏奖励挑战的生产问题中提升了性能。对于低层智能体，设计了一种基于路径规划的空间感知方法（SAP），用于将任务分配给合适的人机资源，从而实现相应的顺序子任务。我们在3D模拟器中针对复杂实时生产过程进行了实验，结果表明所提出的EBQ&SAP方法能有效解决复杂动态生产过程中的人机TPA问题。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for efficient human-robot collaboration in dynamic manufacturing, where spatial information and real-time task allocation are critical challenges, this paper proposes a hierarchical algorithm. The method decomposes tasks and employs a high-level agent using an efficient buffer-based deep Q-learning (EBQ) for planning and a low-level agent using a spatial-aware path planning (SAP) method for allocation. Experimental results in a 3D simulator show that the combined EBQ&SAP approach effectively handles task planning and allocation in complex, real-time production processes, reducing training time and improving performance.
针对动态制造中人机协作中空间信息和实时任务分配的挑战，本文提出了一种分层算法。该方法将任务分解，采用高层智能体基于高效缓冲深度Q学习进行规划，低层智能体基于空间感知路径规划方法进行分配。在3D模拟器中的实验结果表明，所提出的EBQ&SAP方法能有效处理复杂实时生产过程中的任务规划与分配问题，减少了训练时间并提升了性能。
Safe reinforcement learning with online filtering for fatigue-predictive human-robot task planning and allocation in production
Authors: Jintao Xue, Xiao Li, Nianmin Zhang
Venue: Volume 84, February 2026, Pages 561-583
First: 2026-04-14T12:38:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T12:38:21+00:00
Comments: This is the accepted manuscript of an article accepted for publication in \textit{Journal of Manufacturing Systems (Elsevier)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Human-robot collaborative manufacturing, a core aspect of Industry 5.0, emphasizes ergonomics to enhance worker well-being. This paper addresses the dynamic human-robot task planning and allocation (HRTPA) problem, which involves determining when to perform tasks and who should execute them to maximize efficiency while ensuring workers' physical fatigue remains within safe limits. The inclusion of fatigue constraints, combined with production dynamics, significantly increases the complexity of the HRTPA problem. Traditional fatigue-recovery models in HRTPA often rely on static, predefined hyperparameters. However, in practice, human fatigue sensitivity varies daily due to factors such as changed work conditions and insufficient sleep. To better capture this uncertainty, we treat fatigue-related parameters as inaccurate and estimate them online based on observed fatigue progression during production. To address these challenges, we propose PF-CD3Q, a safe reinforcement learning (safe RL) approach that integrates the particle filter with constrained dueling double deep Q-learning for real-time fatigue-predictive HRTPA. Specifically, we first develop PF-based estimators to track human fatigue and update fatigue model parameters in real-time. These estimators are then integrated into CD3Q by making task-level fatigue predictions during decision-making and excluding tasks that exceed fatigue limits, thereby constraining the action space and formulating the problem as a constrained Markov decision process (CMDP).
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于在线滤波的安全强化学习在生产中用于疲劳预测的人机任务规划与分配
人机协同制造作为工业5.0的核心要素，强调通过人机工程学提升劳动者福祉。本文研究动态人机任务规划与分配问题，旨在确定任务执行时机与执行主体，以在确保劳动者生理疲劳处于安全限值内的同时实现效率最大化。疲劳约束与生产动态性的结合显著增加了该问题的复杂性。传统人机任务规划中的疲劳恢复模型常依赖静态预设超参数，然而实践中，人类疲劳敏感性会因工作条件变化、睡眠不足等因素逐日波动。为更好捕捉这种不确定性，我们将疲劳相关参数视为不精确量，并依据生产过程中观测到的疲劳进展进行在线估计。为此，我们提出PF-CD3Q——一种融合粒子滤波与约束对决双深度Q学习的安全强化学习方法，用于实时疲劳预测的人机任务规划。具体而言，我们首先构建基于粒子滤波的估计器以追踪人体疲劳状态并实时更新疲劳模型参数；随后将这些估计器集成至CD3Q框架中，通过在决策时进行任务级疲劳预测、排除超限任务来约束动作空间，从而将问题建模为约束马尔可夫决策过程。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for ergonomic human-robot collaboration in Industry 5.0, this paper tackles the dynamic task planning and allocation problem to maximize efficiency while keeping worker fatigue within safe limits, a challenge complicated by daily variations in human fatigue sensitivity. The proposed method, PF-CD3Q, is a safe reinforcement learning approach that integrates a particle filter for online estimation of fatigue model parameters with a constrained dueling double deep Q-learning algorithm; this allows for real-time tracking of fatigue and updating of its predictive model. The main experimental results demonstrate that the integrated system successfully formulates the problem as a constrained Markov decision process, making task-level fatigue predictions to exclude unsafe actions and dynamically allocate tasks in a way that respects fatigue constraints during production.
本文的动机源于工业5.0中对符合人体工程学的人机协作的需求，旨在解决动态的人机任务规划与分配问题，以在确保工人疲劳度处于安全限值内的同时最大化效率，该问题因人体疲劳敏感性的日常波动而变得复杂。所提出的方法PF-CD3Q是一种安全强化学习方法，它将用于在线估计疲劳模型参数的粒子滤波器与约束对决双深度Q学习算法相结合，从而实现了对疲劳的实时跟踪和预测模型的更新。主要实验结果表明，该集成系统成功地将问题构建为约束马尔可夫决策过程，通过任务级疲劳预测来排除不安全动作，并在生产过程中以尊重疲劳约束的方式动态分配任务。
PromptEcho: Annotation-Free Reward from Vision-Language Models for Text-to-Image Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jinlong Liu, Wanggui He, Peng Zhang, Mushui Liu, Hao Jiang, Pipei Huang
First: 2026-04-14T12:21:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T12:21:15+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) can improve the prompt following capability of text-to-image (T2I) models, yet obtaining high-quality reward signals remains challenging: CLIP Score is too coarse-grained, while VLM-based reward models (e.g., RewardDance) require costly human-annotated preference data and additional fine-tuning. We propose PromptEcho, a reward construction method that requires \emph{no} annotation and \emph{no} reward model training. Given a generated image and a guiding query, PromptEcho computes the token-level cross-entropy loss of a frozen VLM with the original prompt as the label, directly extracting the image-text alignment knowledge encoded during VLM pretraining. The reward is deterministic, computationally efficient, and improves automatically as stronger open-source VLMs become available. For evaluation, we develop DenseAlignBench, a benchmark of concept-rich dense captions for rigorously testing prompt following capability. Experimental results on two state-of-the-art T2I models (Z-Image and QwenImage-2512) demonstrate that PromptEcho achieves substantial improvements on DenseAlignBench (+26.8pp / +16.2pp net win rate), along with consistent gains on GenEval, DPG-Bench, and TIIFBench without any task-specific training. Ablation studies confirm that PromptEcho comprehensively outperforms inference-based scoring with the same VLM, and that reward quality scales with VLM size. We will open-source the trained models and the DenseAlignBench.
中文标题/摘要
标题：PromptEcho：基于视觉语言模型的无标注奖励机制用于文本到图像强化学习
强化学习（RL）能够提升文本到图像（T2I）模型的提示跟随能力，但获取高质量奖励信号仍具挑战：CLIP分数过于粗粒度，而基于视觉语言模型（VLM）的奖励模型（如RewardDance）需要昂贵的人工标注偏好数据及额外微调。本文提出PromptEcho——一种无需标注且无需奖励模型训练的奖励构建方法。给定生成图像与引导查询，PromptEcho通过计算冻结VLM以原始提示为标签的词元级交叉熵损失，直接提取VLM预训练阶段编码的图像-文本对齐知识。该奖励机制具有确定性、计算高效性，并能随更强开源VLM的出现自动提升。为进行评估，我们开发了DenseAlignBench——一个包含丰富概念的密集描述基准，用于严格测试提示跟随能力。在两个前沿T2I模型（Z-Image与QwenImage-2512）上的实验表明，PromptEcho在DenseAlignBench上实现显著提升（净胜率+26.8pp/+16.2pp），并在GenEval、DPG-Bench和TIIFBench基准上取得一致增益，且无需任何任务特定训练。消融研究证实：PromptEcho全面优于使用相同VLM的基于推理的评分方法，且奖励质量随VLM规模扩展而提升。我们将开源训练模型与DenseAlignBench。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for PromptEcho is to address the challenge of obtaining high-quality reward signals for reinforcement learning in text-to-image models, as existing methods like CLIP Score are too coarse and VLM-based reward models require costly human annotations and fine-tuning. The method introduces an annotation-free reward construction technique that computes the token-level cross-entropy loss of a frozen vision-language model using the original prompt as a label, directly leveraging the VLM's pretrained image-text alignment knowledge without additional training. Experimental results on DenseAlignBench and other benchmarks show that PromptEcho achieves significant improvements, such as +26.8pp and +16.2pp net win rates on state-of-the-art T2I models, with ablation studies confirming its superiority over inference-based scoring and scalability with VLM size.
PromptEcho的动机是解决文本到图像模型中强化学习奖励信号获取的挑战，因为现有方法如CLIP Score过于粗糙，而基于视觉语言模型的奖励模型需要昂贵的人工标注和微调。该方法提出了一种无需标注的奖励构建技术，通过计算冻结视觉语言模型的令牌级交叉熵损失，以原始提示作为标签，直接利用VLM预训练中的图像-文本对齐知识，无需额外训练。在DenseAlignBench等基准上的实验结果表明，PromptEcho在先进T2I模型上实现了显著提升，例如净胜率分别增加26.8个百分点和16.2个百分点，消融研究证实其优于基于推理的评分方法，且奖励质量随VLM规模扩展而提升。
Learning Chain Of Thoughts Prompts for Predicting Entities, Relations, and even Literals on Knowledge Graphs
Authors: Alkid Baci, Luke Friedrichs, Caglar Demir, N'Dah Jean Kouagou, Axel-Cyrille Ngonga Ngomo
First: 2026-04-14T12:21:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T12:21:15+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Knowledge graph embedding (KGE) models perform well on link prediction but struggle with unseen entities, relations, and especially literals, limiting their use in dynamic, heterogeneous graphs. In contrast, pretrained large language models (LLMs) generalize effectively through prompting. We reformulate link prediction as a prompt learning problem and introduce RALP, which learns string-based chain-of-thought (CoT) prompts as scoring functions for triples. Using Bayesian Optimization through MIPRO algorithm, RALP identifies effective prompts from fewer than 30 training examples without gradient access. At inference, RALP predicts missing entities, relations or whole triples and assigns confidence scores based on the learned prompt. We evaluate on transductive, numerical, and OWL instance retrieval benchmarks. RALP improves state-of-the-art KGE models by over 5% MRR across datasets and enhances generalization via high-quality inferred triples. On OWL reasoning tasks with complex class expressions (e.g., $\exists hasChild.Female$, $\geq 5 \; hasChild.Female$), it achieves over 88% Jaccard similarity. These results highlight prompt-based LLM reasoning as a flexible alternative to embedding-based methods. We release our implementation, training, and evaluation pipeline as open source: https://github.com/dice-group/RALP .
中文标题/摘要
标题：学习思维链提示以预测知识图谱中的实体、关系乃至字面量
知识图谱嵌入模型在链接预测上表现良好，但难以处理未见过的实体、关系，尤其是字面量，限制了其在动态异构图中的应用。相比之下，预训练大语言模型通过提示能有效泛化。我们将链接预测重构为提示学习问题，提出RALP方法，通过学习基于字符串的思维链提示作为三元组评分函数。通过MIPRO算法进行贝叶斯优化，RALP仅需不足30个训练样本即可识别有效提示，无需梯度访问。在推理阶段，RALP能预测缺失的实体、关系或完整三元组，并根据学习到的提示分配置信度。我们在传导式、数值型和OWL实例检索基准上评估，RALP将最先进知识图谱嵌入模型的平均倒数排名提升超过5%，并通过高质量推断三元组增强泛化能力。在涉及复杂类表达式的OWL推理任务中，其杰卡德相似度超过88%。这些结果表明基于提示的大语言模型推理可作为嵌入方法的灵活替代方案。我们已开源实现代码、训练及评估流程：https://github.com/dice-group/RALP。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitations of knowledge graph embedding (KGE) models, which struggle with unseen entities, relations, and literals in dynamic graphs, by leveraging the generalization capabilities of pretrained large language models (LLMs). The method introduces RALP, a framework that reformulates link prediction as a prompt learning problem, using Bayesian Optimization via the MIPRO algorithm to learn chain-of-thought (CoT) prompts as scoring functions from fewer than 30 training examples without gradient access. Experimental results show that RALP improves state-of-the-art KGE models by over 5% in mean reciprocal rank (MRR) across transductive and numerical benchmarks, achieves over 88% Jaccard similarity on OWL reasoning tasks with complex class expressions, and enhances generalization through high-quality inferred triples, demonstrating prompt-based LLM reasoning as a flexible alternative to embedding-based methods.
本文针对知识图谱嵌入（KGE）模型在动态图中处理未见实体、关系和字面值方面的局限性，利用预训练大语言模型（LLM）的泛化能力，提出了一种新方法。该方法引入了RALP框架，将链接预测重新定义为提示学习问题，通过MIPRO算法进行贝叶斯优化，从少于30个训练样本中学习基于链式思维（CoT）的提示作为评分函数，无需梯度访问。实验结果表明，RALP在传导性和数值基准测试中将最先进KGE模型的平均倒数排名（MRR）提高了超过5%，在涉及复杂类表达式的OWL推理任务中实现了超过88%的杰卡德相似度，并通过高质量推断三元组增强了泛化能力，证明了基于提示的LLM推理是嵌入方法的灵活替代方案。
Contextual Multi-Task Reinforcement Learning for Autonomous Reef Monitoring
Authors: Melvin Laux, Yi-Ling Liu, Rina Alo, Sören Töpper, Mariela De Lucas Alvarez, Frank Kirchner, Rebecca Adam
First: 2026-04-14T12:16:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T12:16:56+00:00
Comments: To be published in IEEE OCEANS 2026 (Sanya) conference proceedings
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Although autonomous underwater vehicles promise the capability of marine ecosystem monitoring, their deployment is fundamentally limited by the difficulty of controlling vehicles under highly uncertain and non-stationary underwater dynamics. To address these challenges, we employ a data-driven reinforcement learning approach to compensate for unknown dynamics and task variations.Traditional single-task reinforcement learning has a tendency to overfit the training environment, thus, limit the long-term usefulness of the learnt policy. Hence, we propose to use a contextual multi-task reinforcement learning paradigm instead, allowing us to learn controllers that can be reused for various tasks, e.g., detecting oysters in one reef and detecting corals in another. We evaluate whether contextual multi-task reinforcement learning can efficiently learn robust and generalisable control policies for autonomous underwater reef monitoring. We train a single context-dependent policy that is able to solve multiple related monitoring tasks in a simulated reef environment in HoloOcean. In our experiments, we empirically evaluate the contextual policies regarding sample-efficiency, zero-shot generalisation to unseen tasks, and robustness to varying water currents. By utilising multi-task reinforcement learning, we aim to improve the training effectiveness, as well as the reusability of learnt policies to take a step towards more sustainable procedures in autonomous reef monitoring.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向自主珊瑚礁监测的情境多任务强化学习
尽管自主水下航行器具备海洋生态系统监测的潜力，但其部署因高度不确定和非平稳的水下动力学环境中的控制难题而受到根本限制。为应对这些挑战，我们采用数据驱动的强化学习方法以补偿未知动力学和任务变化。传统单任务强化学习易对训练环境过拟合，从而限制所学策略的长期有效性。因此，我们提出采用情境多任务强化学习范式，以学习可重用于不同任务的控制器，例如在一个礁区检测牡蛎，在另一礁区检测珊瑚。我们评估情境多任务强化学习能否高效学习适用于自主水下珊瑚礁监测的鲁棒且可泛化的控制策略。我们在HoloOcean模拟礁环境中训练单一情境依赖策略，使其能解决多个相关监测任务。实验中，我们从样本效率、对未见任务的零样本泛化能力及对变化水流的鲁棒性等方面实证评估情境策略。通过利用多任务强化学习，我们旨在提升训练效率及所学策略的可重用性，从而推动自主珊瑚礁监测向更可持续的方向发展。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to overcome the limitations of autonomous underwater vehicles in marine monitoring, which are hindered by uncertain and non-stationary underwater dynamics and the tendency of single-task reinforcement learning to overfit. The method employs a contextual multi-task reinforcement learning approach to learn a single context-dependent policy capable of handling multiple related tasks, such as detecting different marine species. Experimental results in a simulated reef environment demonstrate that this approach improves sample efficiency, enables zero-shot generalization to unseen tasks, and enhances robustness to varying water currents, thereby promoting more sustainable and reusable autonomous monitoring solutions.

KnowRL: Boosting LLM Reasoning via Reinforcement Learning with Minimal-Sufficient Knowledge Guidance
Authors: Linhao Yu, Tianmeng Yang, Siyu Ding, Renren Jin, Naibin Gu, Xiangzhao Hao, Shuaiyi Nie, Deyi Xiong, Weichong Yin, Yu Sun, Hua Wu
First: 2026-04-14T11:53:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T11:53:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
RLVR improves reasoning in large language models, but its effectiveness is often limited by severe reward sparsity on hard problems. Recent hint-based RL methods mitigate sparsity by injecting partial solutions or abstract templates, yet they typically scale guidance by adding more tokens, which introduce redundancy, inconsistency, and extra training overhead. We propose \textbf{KnowRL} (Knowledge-Guided Reinforcement Learning), an RL training framework that treats hint design as a minimal-sufficient guidance problem. During RL training, KnowRL decomposes guidance into atomic knowledge points (KPs) and uses Constrained Subset Search (CSS) to construct compact, interaction-aware subsets for training. We further identify a pruning interaction paradox -- removing one KP may help while removing multiple such KPs can hurt -- and explicitly optimize for robust subset curation under this dependency structure. We train KnowRL-Nemotron-1.5B from OpenMath-Nemotron-1.5B. Across eight reasoning benchmarks at the 1.5B scale, KnowRL-Nemotron-1.5B consistently outperforms strong RL and hinting baselines. Without KP hints at inference, KnowRL-Nemotron-1.5B reaches 70.08 average accuracy, already surpassing Nemotron-1.5B by +9.63 points; with selected KPs, performance improves to 74.16, establishing a new state of the art at this scale. The model, curated training data, and code are publicly available at https://github.com/Hasuer/KnowRL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：KnowRL：通过强化学习与最小充分知识引导提升大语言模型推理能力
RLVR虽能提升大语言模型的推理能力，但其在难题上的效果常受严重奖励稀疏性限制。近期基于提示的强化学习方法通过注入部分解或抽象模板缓解稀疏性，但通常通过增加标记数量来扩展引导，这会引入冗余、不一致性和额外训练开销。我们提出\textbf{KnowRL}（知识引导的强化学习），这是一个将提示设计视为最小充分引导问题的强化学习训练框架。在强化学习训练期间，KnowRL将引导分解为原子知识点（KP），并利用约束子集搜索（CSS）构建紧凑、交互感知的子集进行训练。我们进一步发现一种剪枝交互悖论——移除单个知识点可能有益，而移除多个此类知识点反而有害——并在此依赖结构下显式优化鲁棒子集筛选。我们从OpenMath-Nemotron-1.5B训练得到KnowRL-Nemotron-1.5B。在1.5B规模的八个推理基准测试中，KnowRL-Nemotron-1.5B始终优于强化的强化学习和提示基线方法。在推理阶段不使用知识点提示时，KnowRL-Nemotron-1.5B达到70.08的平均准确率，已超越Nemotron-1.5B达9.63分；使用精选知识点后，性能提升至74.16，创造了该规模下的新最优水平。模型、精选训练数据及代码已公开于https://github.com/Hasuer/KnowRL。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind KnowRL is to enhance the reasoning capabilities of large language models (LLMs) by addressing the reward sparsity issue in reinforcement learning (RL) for hard problems, where existing hint-based methods often introduce redundancy and inefficiency by scaling guidance through additional tokens. The method involves a novel RL framework that treats hint design as a minimal-sufficient guidance problem, decomposing guidance into atomic knowledge points (KPs) and using Constrained Subset Search (CSS) to construct compact, interaction-aware subsets for training, while explicitly optimizing for robust subset curation to handle dependency structures like the pruning interaction paradox. Experimental results show that KnowRL-Nemotron-1.5B, trained from OpenMath-Nemotron-1.5B, outperforms strong RL and hinting baselines across eight reasoning benchmarks at the 1.5B scale, achieving an average accuracy of 70.08 without KP hints at inference (a +9.63 point improvement over the base model) and 74.16 with selected KPs, setting a new state-of-the-art performance at this scale.
KnowRL的动机是通过解决强化学习在困难问题中的奖励稀疏性问题来提升大语言模型的推理能力，现有基于提示的方法通常通过增加标记来扩展指导，但会引入冗余和低效。该方法提出了一种新颖的强化学习框架，将提示设计视为最小充分指导问题，将指导分解为原子知识点，并利用约束子集搜索构建紧凑、交互感知的训练子集，同时显式优化鲁棒子集选择以处理如剪枝交互悖论等依赖结构。实验结果表明，基于OpenMath-Nemotron-1.5B训练的KnowRL-Nemotron-1.5B在1.5B规模的八个推理基准测试中均优于强化的RL和提示基线，在推理时不使用知识点提示的平均准确率达到70.08（比基础模型提升9.63分），使用选定知识点后性能提升至74.16，在此规模上建立了新的最先进水平。
SOAR: Self-Correction for Optimal Alignment and Refinement in Diffusion Models
Authors: You Qin, Linqing Wang, Hao Fei, Roger Zimmermann, Liefeng Bo, Qinglin Lu, Chunyu Wang
First: 2026-04-14T11:45:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T11:45:15+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The post-training pipeline for diffusion models currently has two stages: supervised fine-tuning (SFT) on curated data and reinforcement learning (RL) with reward models. A fundamental gap separates them. SFT optimizes the denoiser only on ground-truth states sampled from the forward noising process; once inference deviates from these ideal states, subsequent denoising relies on out-of-distribution generalization rather than learned correction, exhibiting the same exposure bias that afflicts autoregressive models, but accumulated along the denoising trajectory instead of the token sequence. RL can in principle address this mismatch, yet its terminal reward signal is sparse, suffers from credit-assignment difficulty, and risks reward hacking. We propose SOAR (Self-Correction for Optimal Alignment and Refinement), a bias-correction post-training method that fills this gap. Starting from a real sample, SOAR performs a single stop-gradient rollout with the current model, re-noises the resulting off-trajectory state, and supervises the model to steer back toward the original clean target. The method is on-policy, reward-free, and provides dense per-timestep supervision with no credit-assignment problem. On SD3.5-Medium, SOAR improves GenEval from 0.70 to 0.78 and OCR from 0.64 to 0.67 over SFT, while simultaneously raising all model-based preference scores. In controlled reward-specific experiments, SOAR surpasses Flow-GRPO in final metric value on both aesthetic and text-image alignment tasks, despite having no access to a reward model. Since SOAR's base loss subsumes the standard SFT objective, it can directly replace SFT as a stronger first post-training stage after pretraining, while remaining fully compatible with subsequent RL alignment.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SOAR：扩散模型中的自校正优化对齐与精炼方法
当前扩散模型的后训练流程包含两个阶段：基于精选数据的监督微调（SFT）和基于奖励模型的强化学习（RL）。两者之间存在根本性断层：SFT仅针对前向加噪过程采样的真实状态优化去噪器，一旦推理过程偏离这些理想状态，后续去噪便依赖分布外泛化而非习得性校正，这暴露了与自回归模型类似的曝光偏差问题（偏差沿去噪轨迹而非词元序列累积）。RL理论上可解决此错配，但其终端奖励信号稀疏、存在信用分配难题且易受奖励攻击。我们提出SOAR（自校正优化对齐与精炼）——一种填补该断层的偏差校正后训练方法。该方法从真实样本出发，使用当前模型执行单次梯度截断推演，对生成的轨迹外状态重新加噪，并监督模型使其回归原始干净目标。该方法具有同策略、无奖励依赖、提供密集的逐时间步监督且无需信用分配的特点。在SD3.5-Medium模型上，SOAR将GenEval分数从0.70提升至0.78，OCR分数从0.64提升至0.67，同时全面提升了基于模型的偏好评分。在受控的奖励专项实验中，SOAR在美学与图文对齐任务上的最终指标均超越Flow-GRPO，且无需奖励模型参与。由于SOAR的基础损失函数包含标准SFT目标，其可直接替代SFT作为预训练后更强大的首阶段后训练方法，同时完全兼容后续的RL对齐流程。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses a gap in the post-training pipeline for diffusion models, where supervised fine-tuning (SFT) suffers from exposure bias due to reliance on ground-truth states, and reinforcement learning (RL) faces issues like sparse rewards and credit assignment. To bridge this, the authors propose SOAR, a self-correction method that performs on-policy, reward-free rollouts: starting from a real sample, it generates an off-trajectory state via a stop-gradient rollout, re-noises it, and supervises the model to correct back to the original target, providing dense per-timestep guidance. Experiments on SD3.5-Medium show SOAR improves metrics like GenEval from 0.70 to 0.78 and OCR from 0.64 to 0.67 over SFT, while also outperforming reward-based methods like Flow-GRPO on aesthetic and alignment tasks without using reward models, making it a viable replacement for SFT in post-training.
本文针对扩散模型后训练流程中的缺陷提出改进，其中监督微调（SFT）因依赖真实状态而存在暴露偏差，而强化学习（RL）则面临奖励稀疏和信用分配困难等问题。为此，作者提出了SOAR方法，这是一种自校正技术，通过无奖励的在线策略执行：从真实样本出发，利用停止梯度展开生成偏离轨迹的状态，重新加噪后监督模型校正回原始目标，从而提供密集的每步指导。在SD3.5-Medium上的实验表明，SOAR将GenEval从0.70提升至0.78，OCR从0.64提升至0.67，优于SFT；同时，在审美和图文对齐任务上，即使不使用奖励模型，其表现也超过了基于奖励的方法如Flow-GRPO，因此可作为后训练中替代SFT的更强初始阶段。
Hybrid-AIRL: Enhancing Inverse Reinforcement Learning with Supervised Expert Guidance
Authors: Bram Silue, Santiago Amaya-Corredor, Patrick Mannion, Lander Willem, Pieter Libin
First: 2025-11-26T13:04:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-14T09:58:45+00:00
Comments: Comments: 13 pages, 5 figures, 1 table. Code: https://github.com/silue-dev/hairl. Accepted at ESANN 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Adversarial Inverse Reinforcement Learning (AIRL) has shown promise in addressing the sparse reward problem in reinforcement learning (RL) by inferring dense reward functions from expert demonstrations. However, its performance in highly complex, imperfect-information settings remains largely unexplored. To explore this gap, we evaluate AIRL in the context of Heads-Up Limit Hold'em (HULHE) poker, a domain characterized by sparse, delayed rewards and significant uncertainty. In this setting, we find that AIRL struggles to infer a sufficiently informative reward function. To overcome this limitation, we contribute Hybrid-AIRL (H-AIRL), an extension that enhances reward inference and policy learning by incorporating a supervised loss derived from expert data and a stochastic regularization mechanism. We evaluate H-AIRL on a carefully selected set of Gymnasium benchmarks and the HULHE poker setting. Additionally, we analyze the learned reward function through visualization to gain deeper insights into the learning process. Our experimental results show that H-AIRL achieves higher sample efficiency and more stable learning compared to AIRL. This highlights the benefits of incorporating supervised signals into inverse RL and establishes H-AIRL as a promising framework for tackling challenging, real-world settings.
中文标题/摘要
标题：混合对抗逆强化学习：通过监督式专家指导增强逆强化学习
对抗逆强化学习（AIRL）通过从专家示范中推断密集奖励函数，在解决强化学习中的稀疏奖励问题方面展现出潜力。然而，其在高度复杂、信息不完善场景下的性能尚未得到充分探索。为填补这一空白，我们在“单挑限注德州扑克”（HULHE）这一具有奖励稀疏、延迟且不确定性显著特点的领域中评估AIRL。在此场景下，我们发现AIRL难以推断出足够信息量的奖励函数。为克服此局限，我们提出混合对抗逆强化学习（H-AIRL），该扩展方法通过引入源自专家数据的监督损失函数和随机正则化机制，增强了奖励推断与策略学习能力。我们在精选的Gymnasium基准测试集和HULHE扑克场景中对H-AIRL进行评估，并通过可视化分析习得的奖励函数以深入理解学习过程。实验结果表明，相较于AIRL，H-AIRL实现了更高的样本效率和更稳定的学习性能，这凸显了将监督信号融入逆强化学习的优势，并确立了H-AIRL作为应对复杂现实场景的有效框架。

The method introduces Hybrid-AIRL (H-AIRL), which enhances AIRL by incorporating a supervised loss from expert demonstrations and a stochastic regularization mechanism to improve reward inference and policy learning.
