The method integrates Control Barrier Functions to enforce safety constraints and employs the Sophia optimizer for stable, adaptive second-order gradient updates. Experimental validation on a nonlinear HPV transmission model shows that SODACER achieves faster convergence, better sample efficiency, and a superior bias-variance trade-off compared to baseline replay methods, while maintaining safe trajectories.
本文旨在实现非线性系统的安全、可扩展最优控制，提出了SODACER强化学习框架，其采用具有自组织自适应聚类的双缓冲区经验回放机制来高效管理经验多样性与冗余。该方法结合控制屏障函数以保证安全约束，并利用Sophia优化器进行自适应的二阶梯度更新以增强稳定性。在非线性HPV传播模型上的实验结果表明，与随机和基于聚类的经验回放方法相比，SODACER实现了更快的收敛速度、更高的样本效率以及更优的偏差-方差权衡，同时确保了系统的安全轨迹。
Enhanced-FQL($λ$), an Efficient and Interpretable RL with novel Fuzzy Eligibility Traces and Segmented Experience Replay
Authors: Mohsen Jalaeian-Farimani, Xiong Xiong, Luca Bascetta
First: 2026-01-07T20:59:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T10:28:16+00:00
Comments: Accepted in ECC26 conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper introduces a fuzzy reinforcement learning framework, Enhanced-FQL($λ$), that integrates novel Fuzzified Eligibility Traces (FET) and Segmented Experience Replay (SER) into fuzzy Q-learning with the Fuzzified Bellman Equation (FBE) for continuous control. The proposed approach employs an interpretable fuzzy rule base instead of complex neural architectures, while maintaining competitive performance through two key innovations: a fuzzified Bellman equation with eligibility traces for stable multi-step credit assignment, and a memory-efficient segment-based experience replay mechanism for enhanced sample efficiency. Theoretical analysis proves the proposed method convergence under standard assumptions. On the Cart--Pole benchmark, Enhanced-FQL($λ$) improves sample efficiency and reduces variance relative to $n$-step fuzzy TD and fuzzy SARSA($λ$), while remaining competitive with the tested DDPG baseline. These results support the proposed framework as an interpretable and computationally compact alternative for moderate-scale continuous control problems.
中文标题/摘要

本文提出一种模糊强化学习框架Enhanced-FQL($λ$)，将新型模糊资格迹与分段经验回放机制融入基于模糊贝尔曼方程的模糊Q学习，用于连续控制任务。该方法采用可解释的模糊规则库替代复杂神经网络架构，通过两项关键创新保持竞争力：采用带资格迹的模糊贝尔曼方程实现稳定的多步信用分配，以及基于分段的高效经验回放机制提升样本效率。理论分析证明该方法在标准假设下具有收敛性。在Cart-Pole基准测试中，相较于$n$步模糊时序差分和模糊SARSA($λ$)，Enhanced-FQL($λ$)提升了样本效率并降低了方差，同时与测试的DDPG基线保持竞争力。结果表明该框架可作为中等规模连续控制问题的可解释且计算紧凑的替代方案。

This paper introduces Enhanced-FQL(λ), a fuzzy reinforcement learning framework designed to offer an interpretable and efficient alternative to neural network-based methods for continuous control tasks. The motivation is to combine the transparency of fuzzy rule bases with competitive performance through two key innovations: Fuzzified Eligibility Traces (FET) for stable multi-step credit assignment and a Segmented Experience Replay (SER) mechanism for improved sample efficiency. The method is theoretically proven to converge. Evolving Many Worlds: Towards Open-Ended Discovery in Petri Dish NCA via Population-Based Training
Authors: Uljad Berdica, Jakob Foerster, Frank Hutter, Arber Zela
First: 2026-04-13T09:56:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T09:56:22+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 12 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The generation of sustained, open-ended complexity from local interactions remains a fundamental challenge in artificial life. Differentiable multi-agent systems, such as Petri Dish Neural Cellular Automata (PD-NCA), exhibit rich self-organization driven purely by spatial competition; however, they are highly sensitive to hyperparameters and frequently collapse into uninteresting patterns and dynamics, such as frozen equilibria or structureless noise. In this paper, we introduce PBT-NCA, a meta-evolutionary algorithm that evolves a population of PD-NCAs subject to a composite objective that rewards both historical behavioral novelty and contemporary visual diversity. Driven by this continuous evolutionary pressure, PBT-NCA spontaneously generates a plethora of emergent lifelike phenomena over extended horizons-a hallmark of true open-endedness. Strikingly, the substrate autonomously discovers diverse morphological survival and self-organization strategies. We observe highly regular, coordinated periodic waves; spore-like scattering where homogeneous groups eject cell-like clusters to colonize distant territories; and fluid, shape-shifting macro-structures that migrate across the substrate, maintaining stable outer boundaries that enclose highly active interiors. By actively penalizing monocultures and dead states, PBT-NCA sustains a state of effective complexity that is neither globally ordered nor globally random, operating persistently at the "edge of chaos".
中文标题/摘要
标题：演化多世界：通过基于种群的训练实现培养皿神经细胞自动机的开放式发现
从局部相互作用中产生持续、开放式的复杂性仍是人工生命领域的根本挑战。可微分多智能体系统，如培养皿神经细胞自动机（PD-NCA），展现出纯粹由空间竞争驱动的丰富自组织行为；然而，它们对超参数高度敏感，常坍缩为无趣的模式与动态，如冻结平衡态或无结构噪声。本文提出PBT-NCA——一种元演化算法，通过复合目标演化PD-NCA种群，该目标同时奖励历史行为新颖性与当前视觉多样性。在持续演化压力驱动下，PBT-NCA在长时间尺度上自发涌现出大量类生命现象，这是真正开放性的标志。引人注目的是，该系统自主发现了多样化的形态生存与自组织策略：我们观察到高度规则、协调的周期性波动；孢子状散射现象中同质群体喷射类细胞团以拓殖遥远区域；以及流体状、形态可变的大型结构在基底上迁移，维持着包裹高活性内部的稳定外边界。通过主动惩罚单一化状态与死亡态，PBT-NCA持续维持着既非全局有序亦非全局随机的有效复杂性状态，持久运行于“混沌边缘”。

Learning to Focus and Precise Cropping: A Reinforcement Learning Framework with Information Gaps and Grounding Loss for MLLMs
Authors: Xuanpu Zhao, Zhentao Tan, Dianmo Sheng, Tianxiang Chen, Yao Liu, Yue Wu, Tao Gong, Qi Chu, Nenghai Yu
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-29T03:18:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T08:50:29+00:00
Comments: Accepted by CVPR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
To enhance the perception and reasoning capabilities of multimodal large language models in complex visual scenes, recent research has introduced agent-based workflows. In these works, MLLMs autonomously utilize image cropping tool to analyze regions of interest for question answering. While existing training strategies, such as those employing supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning, have made significant progress, our empirical analysis reveals a key limitation. We demonstrate the model's strong reliance on global input and its weak dependence on the details within the cropped region. To address this issue, we propose a novel two-stage reinforcement learning framework that does not require trajectory supervision. In the first stage, we introduce the ``Information Gap" mechanism by adjusting the granularity of the global image. This mechanism trains the model to answer questions by focusing on cropped key regions, driven by the information gain these regions provide. The second stage further enhances cropping precision by incorporating a grounding loss, using a small number of bounding box annotations. Experiments show that our method significantly enhances the model's attention to cropped regions, enabling it to achieve state-of-the-art performance on high-resolution visual question-answering benchmarks. Our method provides a more efficient approach for perceiving and reasoning fine-grained details in MLLMs. Code is available at: https://github.com/XuanPu-Z/LFPC.
中文标题/摘要
标题：学习聚焦与精准裁剪：面向多模态大语言模型的含信息间隙与定位损失强化学习框架
为增强多模态大语言模型在复杂视觉场景中的感知与推理能力，近期研究引入了基于智能体的工作流程。这些研究使MLLM能自主利用图像裁剪工具分析感兴趣区域以进行问答。尽管现有训练策略（如采用监督微调与强化学习的方法）已取得显著进展，但我们的实证分析揭示了一个关键局限：模型对全局输入存在强依赖，而对裁剪区域内的细节依赖较弱。为解决此问题，我们提出了一种无需轨迹监督的新型两阶段强化学习框架。第一阶段通过调整全局图像粒度引入“信息间隙”机制，该机制驱动模型基于裁剪关键区域提供的信息增益来聚焦这些区域以回答问题。第二阶段通过引入少量边界框标注的定位损失进一步提升裁剪精度。实验表明，我们的方法显著增强了模型对裁剪区域的注意力，使其在高分辨率视觉问答基准上达到最先进性能。该方法为MLLM感知与推理细粒度细节提供了更高效的途径。代码发布于：https://github.com/XuanPu-Z/LFPC。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the limitation of multimodal large language models (MLLMs) in overly relying on global image context while underutilizing details from cropped regions during agent-based visual question answering. To enhance fine-grained perception, the authors propose a two-stage reinforcement learning framework without trajectory supervision. The first stage employs an "Information Gap" mechanism, which trains the model to focus on cropped key regions by strategically reducing the granularity of the global image, thereby incentivizing reliance on local details. The second stage incorporates a grounding loss using minimal bounding box annotations to further improve cropping precision. Experimental results demonstrate that this method significantly boosts the model's attention to cropped regions, achieving state-of-the-art performance on high-resolution visual question-answering benchmarks.
本文针对多模态大语言模型在基于智能体的视觉问答中过度依赖全局图像而忽视裁剪区域细节的问题，提出了一种无需轨迹监督的两阶段强化学习框架以增强细粒度感知。第一阶段引入“信息间隙”机制，通过调整全局图像的粒度，训练模型依赖裁剪关键区域的信息来回答问题；第二阶段则利用少量边界框标注的定位损失进一步提升裁剪精度。实验结果表明，该方法显著增强了模型对裁剪区域的关注度，在高分辨率视觉问答基准上取得了最先进的性能。
CuraLight: Debate-Guided Data Curation for LLM-Centered Traffic Signal Control
Authors: Qing Guo, Xinhang Li, Junyu Chen, Zheng Guo, Shengzhe Xu, Lin Zhang, Lei Li
First: 2026-04-07T10:05:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T08:40:25+00:00
Comments: accepted at IJCNN 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Traffic signal control (TSC) is a core component of intelligent transportation systems (ITS), aiming to reduce congestion, emissions, and travel time. Recent approaches based on reinforcement learning (RL) and large language models (LLMs) have improved adaptivity, but still suffer from limited interpretability, insufficient interaction data, and weak generalization to heterogeneous intersections. This paper proposes CuraLight, an LLM-centered framework where an RL agent assists the fine-tuning of an LLM-based traffic signal controller. The RL agent explores traffic environments and generates high-quality interaction trajectories, which are converted into prompt-response pairs for imitation fine-tuning. A multi-LLM ensemble deliberation system further evaluates candidate signal timing actions through structured debate, providing preference-aware supervision signals for training. Experiments conducted in SUMO across heterogeneous real-world networks from Jinan, Hangzhou, and Yizhuang demonstrate that CuraLight consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, reducing average travel time by 5.34 percent, average queue length by 5.14 percent, and average waiting time by 7.02 percent. The results highlight the effectiveness of combining RL-assisted exploration with deliberation-based data curation for scalable and interpretable traffic signal control.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CuraLight：面向大语言模型交通信号控制的辩论引导数据精炼框架
交通信号控制是智能交通系统的核心组件，旨在缓解拥堵、降低排放、缩短行程时间。基于强化学习和大语言模型的最新方法提升了适应性，但仍存在可解释性有限、交互数据不足、对异构路口泛化能力弱等问题。本文提出CuraLight——一个以大语言模型为中心的框架，其中强化学习智能体辅助微调基于大语言模型的信号控制器。强化学习智能体探索交通环境并生成高质量交互轨迹，将其转化为提示-响应对以进行模仿微调。多语言模型集成审议系统通过结构化辩论评估候选配时方案，为训练提供偏好感知的监督信号。在SUMO中使用济南、杭州、亦庄异构真实路网进行的实验表明，CuraLight持续优于现有最优基线模型，平均行程时间降低5.34%，平均排队长度减少5.14%，平均等待时间下降7.02%。结果凸显了强化学习辅助探索与基于辩论的数据精炼相结合对可扩展、可解释交通信号控制的有效性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of existing reinforcement learning and large language model approaches in traffic signal control, such as poor interpretability, scarce interaction data, and weak generalization to diverse intersections, this paper introduces CuraLight, a framework that uses an RL agent to explore traffic environments and generate high-quality trajectories for fine-tuning an LLM-based controller. The method converts these trajectories into prompt-response pairs and employs a multi-LLM ensemble deliberation system to evaluate signal timing actions through structured debate, providing preference-aware supervision for training. Experimental results in SUMO simulations across real-world networks from Jinan, Hangzhou, and Yizhuang show that CuraLight outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, reducing average travel time by 5.34%, queue length by 5.14%, and waiting time by 7.02%, demonstrating the effectiveness of combining RL-assisted exploration with deliberation-based data curation for scalable and interpretable control.
针对现有基于强化学习和大型语言模型的交通信号控制方法在可解释性、交互数据不足以及对异构路口泛化能力弱等方面的局限，本文提出了CuraLight框架，其中强化学习智能体探索交通环境并生成高质量轨迹，用于微调基于大型语言模型的信号控制器。该方法将轨迹转换为提示-响应对，并采用多大型语言模型集成审议系统，通过结构化辩论评估候选信号配时动作，为训练提供偏好感知的监督信号。在SUMO中使用济南、杭州和亦庄的真实路网进行的实验表明，CuraLight持续优于现有先进基线，平均行程时间减少5.34%，平均排队长度减少5.14%，平均等待时间减少7.02%，结果凸显了结合强化学习辅助探索与基于审议的数据策展对于可扩展且可解释的交通信号控制的有效性。
Curriculum-based Sample Efficient Reinforcement Learning for Robust Stabilization of a Quadrotor
Authors: Fausto Mauricio Lagos Suarez, Akshit Saradagi, Vidya Sumathy, Shruti Kotpaliwar, George Nikolakopoulos
First: 2025-01-30T17:05:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T08:25:27+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 7 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This article introduces a novel sample-efficient curriculum learning (CL) approach for training an end-to-end reinforcement learning (RL) policy for robust stabilization of a Quadrotor. The learning objective is to simultaneously stabilize position and yaw-orientation from random initial conditions through direct control over motor RPMs (end-to-end), while adhering to pre-specified transient and steady-state specifications. This objective, relevant in aerial inspection applications, is challenging for conventional one-stage end-to-end RL, which requires substantial computational resources and lengthy training times. To address this challenge, this article draws inspiration from human-inspired curriculum learning and decomposes the learning objective into a three-stage curriculum that incrementally increases task complexity, while transferring knowledge from one stage to the next. In the proposed curriculum, the policy sequentially learns hovering, the coupling between translational and rotational degrees of freedom, and robustness to random non-zero initial velocities, utilizing a custom reward function and episode truncation conditions. The results demonstrate that the proposed CL approach achieves superior performance compared to a policy trained conventionally in one stage, with the same reward function and hyperparameters, while significantly reducing computational resource needs (samples) and convergence time. The CL-trained policy's performance and robustness are thoroughly validated in a simulation engine (Gym-PyBullet-Drones), under random initial conditions, and in an inspection pose-tracking scenario. A video presenting our results is available at https://youtu.be/9wv6T4eezAU.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于课程学习的样本高效强化学习实现四旋翼鲁棒稳定控制
本文提出一种新颖的样本高效课程学习方法，用于训练端到端强化学习策略以实现四旋翼的鲁棒稳定控制。该学习目标是通过直接控制电机转速（端到端），从随机初始条件同时稳定位置与偏航角，并满足预设的瞬态与稳态性能指标。这一面向空中巡检应用的目标对传统单阶段端到端强化学习具有挑战性，因其需要大量计算资源与漫长训练时间。为解决该问题，本文受人类渐进式学习的启发，将学习目标分解为三阶段课程，逐步提升任务复杂度并实现阶段间知识迁移。在所提课程中，策略通过定制奖励函数与回合截断条件，依次学习悬停控制、平移与旋转自由度耦合关系，以及对随机非零初始速度的鲁棒性。实验结果表明：在相同奖励函数与超参数条件下，相比传统单阶段训练策略，所提课程学习方法在显著降低计算资源需求（样本量）与收敛时间的同时，获得了更优性能。经仿真平台（Gym-PyBullet-Drones）在随机初始条件与巡检姿态跟踪场景中的全面验证，该课程学习训练策略展现出卓越的性能与鲁棒性。成果演示视频详见：https://youtu.be/9wv6T4eezAU。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the challenge of training end-to-end reinforcement learning policies for quadrotor stabilization, which typically demands high computational resources and long training times. The method introduces a sample-efficient curriculum learning approach that decomposes the task into three stages—hovering, coupling of translational and rotational dynamics, and robustness to initial velocities—transferring knowledge between stages to incrementally build complexity. Experimental results in simulation show that this curriculum-based method outperforms conventional one-stage training in performance and robustness while significantly reducing sample requirements and convergence time, validated under random initial conditions and a pose-tracking scenario.
本文针对四旋翼飞行器端到端强化学习策略训练中计算资源需求高、训练时间长的问题，提出了一种基于课程学习的高效样本方法。该方法将学习目标分解为三个阶段——悬停、平移与旋转自由度耦合以及初始速度鲁棒性，通过阶段间知识迁移逐步增加任务复杂度。实验结果表明，在相同奖励函数和超参数下，该课程学习方法在仿真中比传统单阶段训练表现出更优的性能和鲁棒性，同时显著减少了样本需求和收敛时间，并在随机初始条件和姿态跟踪场景中得到了验证。
From Pixels to Digital Agents: An Empirical Study on the Taxonomy and Technological Trends of Reinforcement Learning Environments
Authors: Lijing Luo, Yiben Luo, Alexey Gorbatovski, Sergey Kovalchuk, Xiaodan Liang
First: 2026-03-25T05:56:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T08:15:41+00:00
Comments: 32 pages main text, 18 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The remarkable progress of reinforcement learning (RL) is intrinsically tied to the environments used to train and evaluate artificial agents. Moving beyond traditional qualitative reviews, this work presents a large-scale, data-driven empirical investigation into the evolution of RL environments. By programmatically processing a massive corpus of academic literature and rigorously distilling over 2,000 core publications, we propose a quantitative methodology to map the transition from isolated physical simulations to generalist, language-driven foundation agents. Implementing a novel, multi-dimensional taxonomy, we systematically analyze benchmarks against diverse application domains and requisite cognitive capabilities. Our automated semantic and statistical analysis reveals a profound, data-verified paradigm shift: the bifurcation of the field into a "Semantic Prior" ecosystem dominated by Large Language Models (LLMs) and a "Domain-Specific Generalization" ecosystem. Furthermore, we characterize the "cognitive fingerprints" of these distinct domains to uncover the underlying mechanisms of cross-task synergy, multi-domain interference, and zero-shot generalization. Ultimately, this study offers a rigorous, quantitative roadmap for designing the next generation of Embodied Semantic Simulators, bridging the gap between continuous physical control and high-level logical reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从像素到数字智能体：强化学习环境分类体系与技术趋势的实证研究
强化学习（RL）的显著进展与用于训练和评估智能体的环境密不可分。本研究超越传统的定性综述，对RL环境的演变进行了大规模、数据驱动的实证调查。通过程序化处理海量学术文献并严格提炼超过2000篇核心出版物，我们提出了一种量化方法，以描绘从孤立的物理模拟到通用、语言驱动的基座智能体的转变路径。通过实施一种新颖的多维分类体系，我们系统分析了不同应用领域和所需认知能力对应的基准测试。自动化的语义与统计分析揭示了一个经数据验证的深刻范式转变：该领域正分化为以大型语言模型（LLM）为主导的“语义先验”生态系统和“领域特定泛化”生态系统。此外，我们刻画了这些不同领域的“认知指纹”，以揭示跨任务协同、多领域干扰和零样本泛化的内在机制。最终，本研究为设计下一代具身语义模拟器提供了严谨的量化路线图，弥合了连续物理控制与高层逻辑推理之间的鸿沟。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to move beyond qualitative reviews and understand the evolution of reinforcement learning (RL) environments that underpin agent training, this study conducts a large-scale, data-driven empirical analysis. Scalable Stewardship of an LLM-Assisted Clinical Benchmark with Physician Oversight
Authors: Junze Ye, Daniel Tawfik, Alex J. Goodell, Nikhil V. Kotha, Mark K. Buyyounouski, Mohsen Bayati
First: 2025-12-22T18:59:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T08:00:46+00:00
Comments: Github codebase: https://github.com/junzeye/validate-medcalc-labels
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reference labels for machine-learning benchmarks are increasingly synthesized with LLM assistance, but their reliability remains underexamined. We audit MedCalc-Bench, a clinical benchmark for medical score computation whose labels were partly derived with LLM assistance, and develop a scalable physician-in-the-loop stewardship pipeline to reassess them. At least 27% of test labels are likely erroneous or incomputable. On a 50-instance subset validated by physicians, our recomputed labels agree with physician ground truth 74% of the time (95% CI, 60-84%) versus 20% for the originals (95% CI, 11-33%). Using original labels to evaluate frontier LLMs underestimates accuracy by 16-23 percentage points. In a controlled reinforcement-learning experiment, a model trained on recomputed labels outperforms one trained on originals by 13.5 percentage points (95% CI, 10.6-16.6%) on physician-labeled instances, and this advantage extends to related medical tasks. LLM-assisted benchmarks can propagate systematic errors into both evaluation and post-training unless actively stewarded.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于医生监督的大语言模型辅助临床基准的可扩展管理
机器学习基准的参考标签正日益借助大语言模型合成，但其可靠性仍缺乏检验。本研究对临床医学评分计算基准MedCalc-Bench进行审计（其标签部分由大语言模型生成），并开发了可扩展的医生参与式管理流程进行重评估。测试标签中至少27%可能存在错误或无法计算。在医生验证的50例样本子集中，我们重计算的标签与医生标注真值的吻合率达74%（95% CI 60-84%），而原始标签仅为20%（95% CI 11-33%）。使用原始标签评估前沿大语言模型会低估16-23个百分点的准确率。在对照强化学习实验中，基于重计算标签训练的模型在医生标注样本上比原始标签训练模型提升13.5个百分点（95% CI 10.6-16.6%），该优势可延伸至相关医疗任务。除非实施主动管理，否则大语言模型辅助的基准可能将系统性误差传播至评估及训练后阶段。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by concerns over the reliability of LLM-assisted benchmark labels, this study audits MedCalc-Bench, a clinical benchmark for medical score computation, and develops a scalable physician-in-the-loop stewardship pipeline to reassess its labels. The method involves physician oversight to identify and correct errors, revealing that at least 27% of the original test labels are likely erroneous or incomputable. From Answers to Arguments: Toward Trustworthy Clinical Diagnostic Reasoning with Toulmin-Guided Curriculum Goal-Conditioned Learning
Authors: Chen Zhan, Xiaoyu Tan, Gengchen Ma, Yu-Jie Xiong, Xiaoyan Jiang, Xihe Qiu
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-13T07:49:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T07:49:39+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ACL 2026 (Main Conference)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The integration of Large Language Models (LLMs) into clinical decision support is critically obstructed by their opaque and often unreliable reasoning. In the high-stakes domain of healthcare, correct answers alone are insufficient; clinical practice demands full transparency to ensure patient safety and enable professional accountability. A pervasive and dangerous weakness of current LLMs is their tendency to produce "correct answers through flawed reasoning." This issue is far more than a minor academic flaw; such process errors signal a fundamental lack of robust understanding, making the model prone to broader hallucinations and unpredictable failures when faced with real-world clinical complexity. In this paper, we establish a framework for trustworthy clinical argumentation by adapting the Toulmin model to the diagnostic process. We propose a novel training pipeline: Curriculum Goal-Conditioned Learning (CGCL), designed to progressively train LLM to generate diagnostic arguments that explicitly follow this Toulmin structure. CGCL's progressive three-stage curriculum systematically builds a solid clinical argument: (1) extracting facts and generating differential diagnoses; (2) justifying a core hypothesis while rebutting alternatives; and (3) synthesizing the analysis into a final, qualified conclusion. We validate CGCL using T-Eval, a quantitative framework measuring the integrity of the diagnosis reasoning. Experiments show that our method achieves diagnostic accuracy and reasoning quality comparable to resource-intensive Reinforcement Learning (RL) methods, while offering a more stable and efficient training pipeline.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从答案到论证：基于图尔敏模型的课程目标条件学习实现可信临床诊断推理
大语言模型（LLMs）在临床决策支持中的应用因其不透明且常不可靠的推理而严重受阻。在医疗这一高风险领域，仅提供正确答案远远不够；临床实践要求完全透明以确保患者安全并实现专业问责。当前LLMs普遍存在一个危险缺陷：倾向于通过错误推理得出“正确答案”。这远非细微的学术瑕疵，此类过程错误表明模型缺乏稳健理解力，面对真实临床复杂性时易产生更广泛的幻觉和不可预测的失败。本文通过将图尔敏模型适配至诊断过程，构建了可信临床论证框架。我们提出一种新颖的训练流程：课程目标条件学习（CGCL），旨在渐进式训练LLM生成严格遵循图尔敏结构的诊断论证。CGCL的三阶段渐进课程系统化构建坚实临床论证：（1）提取事实并生成鉴别诊断；（2）论证核心假设同时反驳替代方案；（3）将分析综合为最终限定结论。我们使用T-Eval（一种量化诊断推理完整性的评估框架）验证CGCL。实验表明，本方法在达到与资源密集型强化学习方法相当的诊断准确性和推理质量的同时，提供了更稳定高效的训练流程。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the critical need for transparent and reliable reasoning in clinical decision support, where large language models (LLMs) often produce correct answers through flawed reasoning, this paper introduces a framework for trustworthy clinical argumentation by adapting the Toulmin model to the diagnostic process. The method proposes Curriculum Goal-Conditioned Learning (CGCL), a novel training pipeline that progressively trains LLMs across three stages to generate structured diagnostic arguments: extracting facts and differential diagnoses, justifying a core hypothesis while rebutting alternatives, and synthesizing a qualified conclusion. Experimental results using the T-Eval framework show that CGCL achieves diagnostic accuracy and reasoning quality comparable to resource-intensive reinforcement learning methods, while offering a more stable and efficient training pipeline.
本研究旨在解决大型语言模型在临床决策支持中因推理不透明和不可靠而带来的高风险问题，其动机是模型常通过错误推理得出正确答案，这在医疗领域无法满足透明性和安全性的需求。方法上，论文通过将图尔敏论证模型适配到诊断过程，提出了课程目标条件学习框架，该框架分三个阶段渐进训练模型生成结构化诊断论证：提取事实和生成鉴别诊断、为核心假设提供理由并反驳替代方案、以及综合分析形成最终结论。实验使用T-Eval定量评估框架验证，结果表明该方法在诊断准确性和推理质量上可与资源密集的强化学习方法相媲美，同时提供了更稳定高效的训练流程。
AIM: Intent-Aware Unified world action Modeling with Spatial Value Maps
Authors: Liaoyuan Fan, Zetian Xu, Chen Cao, Wenyao Zhang, Mingqi Yuan, Jiayu Chen
First: 2026-04-13T07:48:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T07:48:58+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Pretrained video generation models provide strong priors for robot control, but existing unified world action models still struggle to decode reliable actions without substantial robot-specific training. We attribute this limitation to a structural mismatch: while video models capture how scenes evolve, action generation requires explicit reasoning about where to interact and the underlying manipulation intent. We introduce AIM, an intent-aware unified world action model that bridges this gap via an explicit spatial interface. Instead of decoding actions directly from future visual representations, AIM predicts an aligned spatial value map that encodes task-relevant interaction structure, enabling a control-oriented abstraction of future dynamics. Built on a pretrained video generation model, AIM jointly models future observations and value maps within a shared mixture-of-transformers architecture. It employs intent-causal attention to route future information to the action branch exclusively through the value representation. We further propose a self-distillation reinforcement learning stage that freezes the video and value branches and optimizes only the action head using dense rewards derived from projected value-map responses together with sparse task-level signals. To support training and evaluation, we construct a simulation dataset of 30K manipulation trajectories with synchronized multi-view observations, actions, and value-map annotations. Experiments on RoboTwin 2.0 benchmark show that AIM achieves a 94.0% average success rate, significantly outperforming prior unified world action baselines. Notably, the improvement is more pronounced in long-horizon and contact-sensitive manipulation tasks, demonstrating the effectiveness of explicit spatial-intent modeling as a bridge between visual world modeling and robot control.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AIM：基于空间价值图表的意图感知统一世界动作建模
预训练视频生成模型为机器人控制提供了强先验，但现有统一世界动作模型仍需大量机器人专属训练才能解码可靠动作。我们将此局限归因于结构错配：视频模型捕捉场景演变，而动作生成需对交互位置与底层操作意图进行显式推理。我们提出AIM，一种意图感知的统一世界动作模型，通过显式空间接口弥合此差距。AIM不直接从未来视觉表征解码动作，而是预测对齐的空间价值图表，编码任务相关的交互结构，实现对未来动态的面向控制抽象。基于预训练视频生成模型，AIM在共享混合Transformer架构中联合建模未来观测与价值图表，采用意图因果注意力机制，使未来信息仅通过价值表征路由至动作分支。我们进一步提出自蒸馏强化学习阶段：冻结视频与价值分支，仅使用投影价值图表响应生成的密集奖励与稀疏任务级信号优化动作头。为支持训练评估，构建包含3万条操作轨迹的仿真数据集，含同步多视角观测、动作及价值图表标注。RoboTwin 2.0基准实验显示，AIM平均成功率94.0%，显著优于先前统一世界动作基线。该改进在长时域与接触敏感操作任务中尤为显著，证明显式空间意图建模作为视觉世界建模与机器人控制桥梁的有效性。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is that pretrained video generation models offer strong priors for robot control, but existing unified world action models fail to decode reliable actions without extensive robot-specific training, due to a structural mismatch between modeling scene evolution and reasoning about interaction locations and manipulation intent. The method introduces AIM, an intent-aware unified world action model that bridges this gap via an explicit spatial interface; instead of decoding actions directly from future visual representations, AIM predicts an aligned spatial value map encoding task-relevant interaction structure, using a shared mixture-of-transformers architecture built on a pretrained video model with intent-causal attention and a self-distillation reinforcement learning stage that optimizes only the action head. The main experimental results, based on a simulation dataset of 30K manipulation trajectories, show that AIM achieves a 94.0% average success rate on the RoboTwin 2.0 benchmark, significantly outperforming prior baselines, with notable improvements in long-horizon and contact-sensitive tasks, demonstrating the effectiveness of explicit spatial-intent modeling.
本研究的动机在于，尽管预训练的视频生成模型为机器人控制提供了强先验，但现有的统一世界动作模型因结构不匹配——即视频模型捕捉场景演变，而动作生成需显式推理交互位置和操作意图——导致在没有大量机器人特定训练时难以解码可靠动作。方法上，提出了AIM这一意图感知的统一世界动作模型，通过显式空间接口弥合此差距；AIM不直接从未来视觉表征解码动作，而是预测一个编码任务相关交互结构的对齐空间价值图，其基于预训练视频模型构建共享混合变换器架构，采用意图因果注意力，并通过自蒸馏强化学习阶段仅优化动作头。主要实验结果基于包含3万条操作轨迹的仿真数据集，显示AIM在RoboTwin 2.0基准测试中达到94.0%的平均成功率，显著优于先前基线，在长时序和接触敏感任务中改进尤为明显，证明了显式空间意图建模作为视觉世界建模与机器人控制桥梁的有效性。
Deep deterministic policy gradient with symmetric data augmentation for lateral attitude tracking control of a fixed-wing aircraft
Authors: Yifei Li, Erik-Jan van Kampen
First: 2024-07-13T08:20:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T07:47:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The symmetry of dynamical systems can be exploited for state-transition prediction and to facilitate control policy optimization. This paper leverages system symmetry to develop sample-efficient offline reinforcement learning (RL) approaches. Under the symmetry assumption for a Markov Decision Process (MDP), a symmetric data augmentation method is proposed. The augmented samples are integrated into the dataset of Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient (DDPG) to enhance its coverage rate of the state-action space. Furthermore, sample utilization efficiency is improved by introducing a second critic trained on the augmented samples, resulting in a dual-critic structure. The aircraft's model is verified to be symmetric, and flight control simulations demonstrate accelerated policy convergence when augmented samples are employed.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于对称数据增强的深度确定性策略梯度在固定翼飞机横侧向姿态跟踪控制中的应用
动力学系统的对称性可用于状态转移预测并促进控制策略优化。本文利用系统对称性开发了样本高效的离线强化学习方法。在马尔可夫决策过程对称性假设下，提出了一种对称数据增强方法。增强样本被整合至深度确定性策略梯度数据集中，以提升其对状态-动作空间的覆盖度。此外，通过引入基于增强样本训练的第二评价器构建双评价器结构，提高了样本利用效率。验证了飞机模型的对称性，飞行控制仿真表明采用增强样本可加速策略收敛。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for sample-efficient offline reinforcement learning, this paper exploits the symmetry of dynamical systems to enhance control policy optimization. The method introduces a symmetric data augmentation technique for Markov Decision Processes, integrating augmented samples into the Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient (DDPG) framework to improve state-action space coverage, and further boosts sample efficiency via a dual-critic structure with a second critic trained on augmented data. Experimental results confirm the symmetry of a fixed-wing aircraft model, and flight control simulations show that using augmented samples accelerates policy convergence.
本文以提高离线强化学习的样本效率为动机，利用动力系统的对称性来优化控制策略。方法提出了一种针对马尔可夫决策过程的对称数据增强技术，将增强样本集成到深度确定性策略梯度（DDPG）框架中以提升状态-动作空间的覆盖度，并通过引入在增强数据上训练的第二个批评器形成双批评器结构，进一步提高了样本利用效率。实验结果验证了固定翼飞机模型的对称性，飞行控制仿真表明，使用增强样本能加速策略收敛。
MADQRL: Distributed Quantum Reinforcement Learning Framework for Multi-Agent Environments
Authors: Abhishek Sawaika, Samuel Yen-Chi Chen, Udaya Parampalli, Rajkumar Buyya
First: 2026-04-13T07:44:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T07:44:23+00:00
Comments: Accepted in QC4C3 Workshop at IEEE QCNC, 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) is one of the most practical ways to learn from real-life use-cases. Motivated from the cognitive methods used by humans makes it a widely acceptable strategy in the field of artificial intelligence. Most of the environments used for RL are often high-dimensional, and traditional RL algorithms becomes computationally expensive and challenging to effectively learn from such systems. Recent advancements in practical demonstration of quantum computing (QC) theories, such as compact encoding, enhanced representation and learning algorithms, random sampling, or the inherent stochastic nature of quantum systems, have opened up new directions to tackle these challenges. Quantum reinforcement learning (QRL) is seeking significant traction over the past few years. However, the current state of quantum hardware is not enough to cater for such high-dimensional environments with complex multi-agent setup. To tackle this issue, we propose a distributed framework for QRL where multiple agents learn independently, distributing the load of joint training from individual machines. Our method works well for environments with disjoint sets of action and observation spaces, but can also be extended to other systems with reasonable approximations. We analyze the proposed method on cooperative-pong environment and our results indicate ~10% improvement from other distribution strategies, and ~5% improvement from classical models of policy representation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MADQRL：面向多智能体环境的分布式量子强化学习框架
强化学习（RL）是从现实用例中学习的最实用方法之一，其受人类认知方法启发，在人工智能领域被广泛接受。多数RL环境具有高维特性，传统RL算法计算成本高昂，难以有效学习。量子计算（QC）理论的实际进展，如紧凑编码、增强表示与学习算法、随机采样或量子系统固有的随机性，为解决这些挑战开辟了新方向。量子强化学习（QRL）近年来备受关注，但当前量子硬件尚不足以应对复杂多智能体设置的高维环境。为此，我们提出一种分布式QRL框架，允许多智能体独立学习，将联合训练负载分配到独立机器上。该方法适用于动作与观测空间不相交的环境，也可通过合理近似扩展到其他系统。我们在合作乒乓球环境中验证了该方法，结果显示其相比其他分布式策略提升约10%，较经典策略表示模型提升约5%。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the computational challenges of traditional reinforcement learning in high-dimensional multi-agent environments and the limitations of current quantum hardware, this paper proposes MADQRL, a distributed quantum reinforcement learning framework. The method distributes the training load across multiple agents that learn independently, particularly suited for environments with disjoint action and observation spaces. Experimental results on a cooperative-pong environment show that the framework achieves approximately a 10% improvement over other distribution strategies and a 5% improvement over classical policy representation models.
本文针对传统强化学习在高维多智能体环境中计算成本高昂的挑战以及当前量子硬件的局限性，提出了MADQRL，一种分布式量子强化学习框架。该方法通过多个智能体独立学习来分担训练负载，尤其适用于动作和观测空间不相交的环境。在合作乒乓球环境上的实验结果表明，该框架相比其他分布式策略提升了约10%，相比经典策略表示模型提升了约5%。
Towards Near-Real-Time Telemetry-Aware Routing with Neural Routing Algorithms
Authors: Andreas Boltres, Niklas Freymuth, Benjamin Schichtholz, Michael König, Gerhard Neumann
First: 2026-04-03T09:51:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T07:28:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Routing algorithms are crucial for efficient computer network operations, and in many settings they must be able to react to traffic bursts within milliseconds. Live telemetry data can provide informative signals to routing algorithms, and recent work has trained neural networks to exploit such signals for traffic-aware routing. Yet, aggregating network-wide information is subject to communication delays, and existing neural approaches either assume unrealistic delay-free global states, or restrict routers to purely local telemetry. This leaves their deployability in real-world environments unclear. We cast telemetry-aware routing as a delay-aware closed-loop control problem and introduce a framework that trains and evaluates neural routing algorithms, while explicitly modeling communication and inference delays. On top of this framework, we propose LOGGIA, a scalable graph neural routing algorithm that predicts log-space link weights from attributed topology-and-telemetry graphs. It utilizes a data-driven pre-training stage, followed by on-policy Reinforcement Learning. Across synthetic and real network topologies, and unseen mixed TCP/UDP traffic sequences, LOGGIA consistently outperforms shortest-path baselines, whereas neural baselines fail once realistic delays are enforced. Our experiments further suggest that neural routing algorithms like LOGGIA perform best when deployed fully locally, i.e., observing network states and inferring actions at every router individually, as opposed to centralized decision making.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向近实时遥测感知路由的神经路由算法研究
路由算法对计算机网络的高效运行至关重要，在许多场景中需能在毫秒级响应流量突发。实时遥测数据可为路由算法提供信息信号，近期研究已训练神经网络利用此类信号实现流量感知路由。然而，全网范围的信息聚合受通信延迟制约，现有神经方法或假设不切实际的无延迟全局状态，或将路由器限制于纯局部遥测，导致其在实际环境中的可部署性不明。本文将遥测感知路由建模为延迟感知闭环控制问题，提出一个训练与评估神经路由算法的框架，并显式建模通信与推理延迟。基于此框架，我们提出LOGGIA——一种可扩展的图神经路由算法，通过属性化拓扑-遥测图预测对数空间链路权重。该算法采用数据驱动的预训练阶段，并结合策略强化学习。在合成与真实网络拓扑及未见过的混合TCP/UDP流量序列测试中，LOGGIA始终优于最短路径基线，而现有神经基线在引入真实延迟后均失效。实验进一步表明，类似LOGGIA的神经路由算法在全局部署（即每个路由器独立观测网络状态并推断行为）时表现最优，而非集中式决策。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of making neural routing algorithms practical for real-world networks by explicitly accounting for communication and inference delays, which prior work often ignored. The authors frame telemetry-aware routing as a delay-aware closed-loop control problem and introduce a framework for training and evaluating neural routing under such constraints. They propose LOGGIA, a scalable graph neural network algorithm that predicts log-space link weights from attributed topology-and-telemetry graphs, using data-driven pre-training followed by on-policy reinforcement learning. Experimental results on synthetic and real topologies with unseen mixed TCP/UDP traffic show that LOGGIA consistently outperforms shortest-path baselines, while other neural methods fail under realistic delays, and further indicate that fully local deployment at each router yields the best performance compared to centralized approaches.
本文针对现有神经路由算法常忽略通信与推理延迟、难以实际部署的问题，将遥测感知路由建模为延迟感知的闭环控制问题，并提出了一个在此约束下训练和评估神经路由的框架。作者设计了LOGGIA这一可扩展的图神经网络算法，它从带属性的拓扑-遥测图中预测对数空间链路权重，采用数据驱动的预训练和策略强化学习相结合的方法。在合成与真实网络拓扑以及未见过的混合TCP/UDP流量序列上的实验表明，LOGGIA持续优于最短路径基线，而其他神经基线在引入现实延迟后失效；结果还提示，在每台路由器上完全本地化部署（而非集中决策）能获得最佳性能。
Record-Remix-Replay: Hierarchical GPU Kernel Optimization using Evolutionary Search
Authors: Daniel Nichols, Konstantinos Parasyris, Caetano Melone, Tal Ben-Nun, Giorgis Georgakoudis, Harshitha Menon
First: 2026-04-13T07:25:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T07:25:12+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As high-performance computing and AI workloads become increasingly dependent on GPUs, maintaining high performance across rapidly evolving hardware generations has become a major challenge. Developers often spend months tuning scientific applications to fully exploit new architectures, navigating a complex optimization space that spans algorithm design, source implementation, compiler flags and pass sequences, and kernel launch parameters. Existing approaches can effectively search parts of this space in isolation, such as launch configurations or compiler settings, but optimizing across the full space still requires substantial human expertise and iterative manual effort. In this paper, we present Record-Remix-Replay (R^3), a hierarchical optimization framework that combines LLM-driven evolutionary search, Bayesian optimization, and record-replay compilation techniques to efficiently explore GPU kernel optimizations from source-level implementation choices down to compiler pass ordering and runtime configuration. By making candidate evaluation fast and scalable, our approach enables practical end-to-end search over optimization dimensions that are typically treated separately. We show that Record-Remix-Replay can optimize full scientific applications better than traditional approaches over kernel parameters and compiler flags, while also being nearly an order of magnitude faster than modern evolutionary search approaches.
中文标题/摘要
标题：记录-重构-重放：基于进化搜索的层次化GPU内核优化框架
随着高性能计算和AI工作负载日益依赖GPU，在快速迭代的硬件代际间保持高性能已成为重大挑战。开发者常需耗费数月调优科学计算应用以充分利用新架构，在涵盖算法设计、源码实现、编译器标志与过程序列、内核启动参数等复杂优化空间中进行探索。现有方法能有效孤立搜索部分空间（如启动配置或编译器设置），但对全空间的优化仍需大量人工专业知识和迭代式手动调优。本文提出记录-重构-重放（R^3）——一种结合LLM驱动进化搜索、贝叶斯优化与记录-重放编译技术的层次化优化框架，能够从源码级实现选择到编译器过程排序及运行时配置，系统探索GPU内核优化方案。通过实现快速可扩展的候选方案评估，本方法支持对传统分立处理的优化维度进行端到端搜索。实验表明，记录-重构-重放框架在优化完整科学计算应用时，不仅优于传统内核参数与编译器标志优化方法，其速度更比现代进化搜索方案提升近一个数量级。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is the significant challenge of maintaining high GPU performance across evolving hardware generations, which currently requires extensive manual tuning of scientific applications across a complex, multi-level optimization space. The method introduces Record-Remix-Replay (R^3), a hierarchical optimization framework that employs LLM-driven evolutionary search combined with Bayesian optimization and record-replay compilation to efficiently explore optimizations from source-level choices down to compiler settings and runtime configurations. The main experimental results demonstrate that R^3 optimizes full scientific applications more effectively than traditional approaches focusing on isolated parameters and is nearly ten times faster than modern evolutionary search methods.

Tree Training: Accelerating Agentic LLMs Training via Shared Prefix Reuse
Authors: Jinghui Wang, Shaojie Wang, Yinghan Cui, Xuxing Chen, Chao Wang, Liang Huang, Xiaojiang Zhang, Junyi Peng, Li Wan, Haotian Zhang, Bin Chen
First: 2025-11-01T05:56:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T06:45:54+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Agentic large language model (LLM) training often involves multi-turn interaction trajectories that branch into multiple execution paths due to concurrent tool use, think-mode, sub-agent, context management and other runtime designs. As a result, the tokens produced by a single task naturally form a tree-structured token trajectory with shared prefixes, rather than a linear sequence. Existing training pipelines linearize such trajectories and treat each branch independently, leading to substantial redundant computation in both forward and backward passes. We derive that averaging the loss over all branches independently is algebraically identical to a per-token weighted loss, where each token's weight equals the fraction of branches passing through it. The problem therefore reduces to computing the log-probability of every token in the prefix tree exactly once, with no repeated computation across shared prefixes: we propose DFS serialization of the tree, which visits every token exactly once, and adapt full-attention and SSM layers to ensure the resulting log-probabilities match independent per-branch calculation exactly. In practice, a single trajectory tree can be too large to fit in GPU memory; we therefore propose Tree Partitioning, a memory-efficient partitioning strategy that splits the tree into subtrees each fitting within GPU memory while preserving high prefix reuse. Together, these contributions form Tree Training, an efficient framework for training LLMs on tree-structured trajectories, achieving up to 6.2x end-to-end training speedup on dense and MOE models for both supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：树形训练：通过共享前缀复用加速智能体大语言模型训练
智能体大语言模型（LLM）训练常涉及多轮交互轨迹，由于并发工具调用、思维模式、子智能体、上下文管理等运行时设计，这些轨迹会分叉为多条执行路径。因此，单个任务生成的词元自然形成具有共享前缀的树形结构轨迹，而非线性序列。现有训练流程将此类轨迹线性化并独立处理每个分支，导致前向与反向传播中存在大量冗余计算。我们推导出：对所有分支损失进行独立平均，在代数上等价于按词元加权损失，其中每个词元的权重等于通过该词元的分支比例。因此问题转化为精确计算前缀树中每个词元的对数概率一次，避免共享前缀的重复计算：我们提出树的深度优先搜索序列化方法，确保每个词元仅被访问一次，并适配全注意力层和状态空间模型层，使生成的对数概率与独立分支计算完全匹配。实践中，单个轨迹树可能过大而无法载入GPU显存；为此我们提出树形分区策略，通过内存高效的分区方法将树拆分为适应GPU显存的子树，同时保持较高的前缀复用率。这些贡献共同构成树形训练框架，可在树形结构轨迹上高效训练LLMs，在监督微调和强化学习中，对稠密模型和混合专家模型实现最高6.2倍的端到端训练加速。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the inefficiency of existing training pipelines that linearize the tree-structured token trajectories arising from agentic LLM interactions, leading to redundant computations. The method introduces Tree Training, which employs DFS serialization to compute each token's log-probability exactly once and adapts attention and SSM layers to align with a per-token weighted loss derived from branch fractions, alongside Tree Partitioning to manage memory constraints by splitting large trees into subtrees. Experimental results demonstrate that this framework achieves up to 6.2x end-to-end training speedup on both dense and MOE models in supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning settings.
本文的动机在于现有训练流程将智能体大语言模型交互中产生的树状令牌轨迹线性化处理，导致大量冗余计算。方法上提出了树训练框架，采用深度优先搜索序列化确保每个令牌的对数概率仅计算一次，并调整注意力与状态空间模型层以匹配基于分支比例的令牌加权损失，同时通过树分区策略将大树分割为适合GPU内存的子结构以提升内存效率。实验结果表明，该框架在监督微调和强化学习任务中，对稠密与混合专家模型实现了最高6.2倍的端到端训练加速。
Rethinking Token-Level Credit Assignment in RLVR: A Polarity-Entropy Analysis
Authors: Yuhang He, Haodong Wu, Siyi Liu, Hongyu Ge, Hange Zhou, Keyi Wu, Zhuo Zheng, Qihong Lin, Zixin Zhong, Yongqi Zhang
First: 2026-04-13T06:32:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T06:32:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has substantially improved the reasoning ability of Large Language Models (LLMs). However, its sparse outcome-based rewards pose a fundamental credit assignment problem. We analyze this problem through the joint lens of reward polarity and token entropy. Our diagnostic tool, the Four Quadrant Decomposition, isolates token updates by polarity and entropy, and controlled ablations show that reasoning improvements concentrate in the high-entropy quadrants. To justify this observation theoretically, we adapt Conditional Mutual Information to the autoregressive RLVR setting and prove that the credit a token can carry is upper-bounded by its entropy. This view yields testable predictions that reasoning gains arise primarily from high-entropy tokens, with unique roles for positive and negative updates. A gradient analysis of GRPO further reveals how uniform reward broadcast dilutes signal at high-entropy positions while over-crediting deterministic tokens. Grounded in these insights, we propose Entropy-Aware Policy Optimization (EAPO) that modulates token-level learning signals accordingly. Extensive experiments demonstrate that EAPO outperforms strong baselines across two model families.
中文标题/摘要
标题：重新审视RLVR中的词元级信用分配：一种极性-熵分析框架
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）显著提升了大型语言模型的推理能力，但其基于稀疏结果的奖励机制引发了根本性的信用分配问题。本研究通过奖励极性与词元熵的双重视角分析该问题：提出的四象限分解工具按极性与熵隔离词元更新，受控消融实验表明推理改进集中于高熵象限。为提供理论依据，我们将条件互信息适配至自回归RLVR场景，证明词元可承载的信用上限受其熵值约束。该视角推导出可验证的预测——推理增益主要源于高熵词元，且正负更新具有独特作用。对GRPO的梯度分析进一步揭示：均匀奖励播散会稀释高熵位置的信号，同时过度赋信于确定性词元。基于这些发现，我们提出熵感知策略优化方法，据此调制词元级学习信号。大量实验证明，该方法在两个模型族系中均优于现有基线。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the credit assignment problem in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), where sparse outcome-based rewards make it difficult to attribute success to specific tokens. The authors analyze the issue through a framework combining reward polarity and token entropy, using a Four Quadrant Decomposition to show experimentally that reasoning improvements are concentrated in high-entropy tokens. They theoretically justify this by adapting Conditional Mutual Information to prove a token's credit capacity is bounded by its entropy, leading to the development of Entropy-Aware Policy Optimization (EAPO), which modulates learning signals based on token entropy and outperforms baselines in experiments.
本文针对可验证奖励强化学习中的信用分配问题展开研究，该问题源于稀疏的结果奖励难以将成功归因于特定词元。作者通过结合奖励极性和词元熵的框架进行分析，利用四象限分解实验表明推理改进集中于高熵词元。他们通过调整条件互信息理论证明了词元的信用承载能力受其熵值上界限制，从而提出了熵感知策略优化方法，该方法根据词元熵调制学习信号，并在实验中超越了现有基线模型。
GroupRank: A Groupwise Paradigm for Effective and Efficient Passage Reranking with LLMs
Authors: Meixiu Long, Duolin Sun, Dan Yang, Yihan Jiao, Lei Liu, Jiahai Wang, BinBin Hu, Yue Shen, Jie Feng, Zhehao Tan, Junjie Wang, Lianzhen Zhong, Jian Wang, Peng Wei, Jinjie Gu
Venue: ACL
First: 2025-11-10T15:25:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T06:26:15+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ACL-Findings 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) have emerged as powerful tools for passage reranking in information retrieval, leveraging their superior reasoning capabilities to address the limitations of conventional models on complex queries. However, current LLM-based reranking paradigms are fundamentally constrained by an efficiency-accuracy trade-off: (1) pointwise methods are efficient but ignore inter-document comparison, yielding suboptimal accuracy; (2) listwise methods capture global context but suffer from context-window constraints and prohibitive inference latency. To address these issues, we propose GroupRank, a novel paradigm that balances flexibility and context awareness. To unlock the full potential of groupwise reranking, we propose an answer-free data synthesis pipeline that fuses local pointwise signals with global listwise rankings. These samples facilitate supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning, with the latter guided by a specialized group-ranking reward comprising ranking-utility and group-alignment. These complementary components synergistically optimize document ordering and score calibration to reflect intrinsic query-document relevance. Experimental results show GroupRank achieves a state-of-the-art 65.2 NDCG@10 on BRIGHT and surpasses baselines by 2.1 points on R2MED, while delivering a 6.4$\times$ inference speedup.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GroupRank：基于分组范式的大语言模型高效段落重排序方法
大语言模型凭借其卓越的推理能力，已成为信息检索中段落重排序的强大工具，能够有效解决传统模型在复杂查询上的局限性。然而，当前基于大语言模型的重排序范式普遍受制于效率与精度的权衡困境：（1）逐点方法效率高但忽略文档间比较，导致精度欠佳；（2）列表方法能捕捉全局上下文，却受限于上下文窗口约束和极高的推理延迟。为此，我们提出GroupRank这一兼顾灵活性与上下文感知能力的新范式。为充分发挥分组重排序的潜力，我们设计了一种无答案数据合成流程，将局部逐点信号与全局列表排序相融合。这些样本支持监督微调与强化学习，后者通过融合排序效用与分组对齐的专用组排序奖励进行引导。两组互补组件协同优化文档排序与分数校准，以反映查询与文档的内在相关性。实验表明，GroupRank在BRIGHT数据集上取得65.2 NDCG@10的最优性能，在R2MED上超越基线2.1个点，同时实现6.4倍的推理加速。

The method introduces a groupwise paradigm that balances flexibility and context awareness, employing an answer-free data synthesis pipeline to combine pointwise signals with listwise rankings for supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning optimized via a group-ranking reward. Experimental results demonstrate state-of-the-art performance, achieving 65.2 NDCG@10 on BRIGHT and a 2.1-point improvement on R2MED, alongside a 6.4× inference speedup.
GroupRank的提出动机源于基于大语言模型的段落重排序中效率与准确性的权衡问题，即点式方法忽略文档间比较而列表式方法受限于上下文窗口和延迟。该方法采用一种平衡灵活性与上下文感知的组式范式，通过无答案数据合成流程融合点式信号与列表式排序，用于监督微调和由组排序奖励优化的强化学习。实验结果表明，该方法在BRIGHT数据集上取得了65.2 NDCG@10的最先进性能，在R2MED上超越基线2.1分，同时实现了6.4倍的推理加速。
RTMC: Step-Level Credit Assignment via Rollout Trees
Authors: Tao Wang, Suhang Zheng, Xiaoxiao Xu
First: 2026-04-13T06:01:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T06:01:51+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-step agentic reinforcement learning benefits from fine-grained credit assignment, yet existing approaches offer limited options: critic-free methods like GRPO assign a uniform advantage to every action in a trajectory, while learned value networks introduce notable overhead and can be fragile under sparse rewards. We observe that group rollouts targeting the same problem often traverse overlapping intermediate states, implicitly forming a tree whose branches diverge at successive decision points. Building on this insight, we introduce Rollout-Tree Monte Carlo (RTMC) advantage estimation, which aggregates return statistics across rollouts sharing a common state to produce per-step Q-values and advantages--without any learned critic. A state-action signature system compresses raw interaction histories into compact, comparable representations, making cross-rollout state matching tractable. On SWE-bench Verified, RTMC improves pass@1 by 3.2 percentage points over GRPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RTMC：基于推演树的分步信用分配方法
多步智能体强化学习受益于细粒度信用分配，但现有方法选择有限：GRPO等无评论家方法对轨迹中每个动作分配均匀优势值，而学习值网络会引入显著开销且在稀疏奖励下表现脆弱。我们观察到，针对同一问题的群体推演常经过重叠的中间状态，隐式形成分支在连续决策点分叉的树结构。基于此发现，我们提出推演树蒙特卡洛优势估计方法，通过聚合共享相同状态的推演回报统计量，生成分步Q值与优势值——无需任何学习型评论家。状态-动作签名系统将原始交互历史压缩为紧凑可比的表征，实现跨推演状态匹配。在SWE-bench Verified基准上，RTMC较GRPO将pass@1指标提升3.2个百分点。

The paper is motivated by the need for fine-grained credit assignment in multi-step reinforcement learning, where existing methods either assign uniform advantages across a trajectory or rely on fragile learned value networks. The proposed method, Rollout-Tree Monte Carlo (RTMC), leverages overlapping intermediate states across group rollouts to form a tree structure, using a state-action signature system to match states and aggregate return statistics without a learned critic, thereby estimating per-step Q-values and advantages. Experimental results on SWE-bench Verified show that RTMC improves pass@1 by 3.2 percentage points over GRPO.
本文的动机在于多步强化学习需要细粒度的信用分配，现有方法要么在整个轨迹中分配均匀的优势值，要么依赖脆弱的学习价值网络。所提出的方法——Rollout-Tree Monte Carlo（RTMC）——利用组间rollout中重叠的中间状态形成树结构，通过状态-动作签名系统匹配状态并聚合回报统计，无需学习评论家，从而估计每步的Q值和优势。在SWE-bench Verified上的实验结果表明，RTMC将pass@1比GRPO提高了3.2个百分点。
Optimal Stability of KL Divergence under Gaussian Perturbations
Authors: Jialu Pan, Yufeng Zhang, Nan Hu, Keqin Li
First: 2026-04-13T05:49:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T05:49:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study the problem of characterizing the stability of Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence under Gaussian perturbations beyond Gaussian families. Existing relaxed triangle inequalities for KL divergence critically rely on the assumption that all involved distributions are Gaussian, which limits their applicability in modern applications such as out-of-distribution (OOD) detection with flow-based generative models. In this paper, we remove this restriction by establishing a sharp stability bound between an arbitrary distribution and Gaussian families under mild moment conditions. Specifically, let $P$ be a distribution with finite second moment, and let $\mathcal{N}_1$ and $\mathcal{N}_2$ be multivariate Gaussian distributions. We show that if $KL(P||\mathcal{N}_1)$ is large and $KL(\mathcal{N}_1||\mathcal{N}_2)$ is at most $ε$, then $KL(P||\mathcal{N}_2) \ge KL(P||\mathcal{N}_1) - O(\sqrtε)$. Moreover, we prove that this $\sqrtε$ rate is optimal in general, even within the Gaussian family. This result reveals an intrinsic stability property of KL divergence under Gaussian perturbations, extending classical Gaussian-only relaxed triangle inequalities to general distributions. The result is non-trivial due to the asymmetry of KL divergence and the absence of a triangle inequality in general probability spaces. As an application, we provide a rigorous foundation for KL-based OOD analysis in flow-based models, removing strong Gaussian assumptions used in prior work. More broadly, our result enables KL-based reasoning in non-Gaussian settings arising in deep learning and reinforcement learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：高斯扰动下KL散度的最优稳定性
本文研究了高斯扰动下Kullback-Leibler（KL）散度稳定性在非高斯分布族中的刻画问题。现有KL散度的松弛三角不等式严格依赖于所有相关分布均为高斯的假设，这限制了其在基于流的生成模型进行分布外（OOD）检测等现代应用中的适用性。本文通过建立任意分布与高斯分布族在温和矩条件下的尖锐稳定性界，突破了这一限制。具体而言，设P为具有有限二阶矩的分布，N1和N2为多元高斯分布。我们证明：若KL(P||N1)较大且KL(N1||N2)至多为ε，则KL(P||N2) ≥ KL(P||N1) - O(√ε)。进一步，我们证明该√ε速率在一般情况下是最优的，即使在高斯分布族内部亦然。这一结果揭示了KL散度在高斯扰动下的内在稳定性，将经典的高斯专属松弛三角不等式推广至一般分布。由于KL散度的非对称性及一般概率空间中三角不等式的缺失，该结论具有非平凡性。作为应用，我们为基于流的模型中KL驱动的OOD分析提供了严格的理论基础，消除了先前工作中强高斯假设的依赖。更广泛而言，本研究使得KL散度推理能够适用于深度学习和强化学习中出现的非高斯场景。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the need to extend the stability analysis of Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence beyond Gaussian distributions, as existing relaxed triangle inequalities are limited to Gaussian families, hindering applications like out-of-distribution detection in flow-based models. The method establishes a sharp stability bound under mild moment conditions, showing that for any distribution P with finite second moment and Gaussian distributions N1 and N2, if KL(P||N1) is large and KL(N1||N2) is at most ε, then KL(P||N2) is at least KL(P||N1) minus O(√ε). The main experimental results confirm that this √ε rate is optimal, even within Gaussian families, revealing an intrinsic stability property and providing a rigorous foundation for KL-based reasoning in non-Gaussian settings such as deep learning and reinforcement learning.
本文的动机在于需要将Kullback-Leibler（KL）散度的稳定性分析扩展到高斯分布之外，因为现有的松弛三角不等式仅限于高斯族，限制了其在基于流的生成模型中进行分布外检测等应用。方法是在温和矩条件下建立尖锐的稳定性界限，表明对于具有有限二阶矩的任意分布P和高斯分布N1与N2，如果KL(P||N1)较大且KL(N1||N2)至多为ε，则KL(P||N2)至少为KL(P||N1)减去O(√ε)。主要实验结果证实了这一√ε速率是最优的，即使在高斯族内也是如此，揭示了KL散度在高斯扰动下的内在稳定性，并为深度学习和强化学习等非高斯设置中的基于KL的推理提供了严格基础。
NimbusGuard: A Novel Framework for Proactive Kubernetes Autoscaling Using Deep Q-Networks
Authors: Chamath Wanigasooriya, Indrajith Ekanayake
First: 2026-04-13T05:32:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T05:32:12+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Cloud native architecture is about building and running scalable microservice applications to take full advantage of the cloud environments. Managed Kubernetes is the powerhouse orchestrating cloud native applications with elastic scaling. However, traditional Kubernetes autoscalers are reactive, meaning the scaling controllers adjust resources only after they detect demand within the cluster and do not incorporate any predictive measures. This can lead to either over-provisioning and increased costs or under-provisioning and performance degradation. We propose NimbusGuard, an open-source, Kubernetes-based autoscaling system that leverages a deep reinforcement learning agent to provide proactive autoscaling. The agents perception is augmented by a Long Short-Term Memory model that forecasts future workload patterns. The evaluations were conducted by comparing NimbusGuard against the built-in scaling controllers, such as Horizontal Pod Autoscaler, and the event-driven autoscaler KEDA. The experimental results demonstrate how NimbusGuard's proactive framework translates into superior performance and cost efficiency compared to existing reactive methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：NimbusGuard：一种基于深度Q网络的主动式Kubernetes自动扩缩容新框架
云原生架构旨在构建和运行可扩展的微服务应用，以充分利用云环境。托管Kubernetes作为编排云原生应用的核心平台，具备弹性扩缩容能力。然而，传统Kubernetes自动扩缩容机制属于被动响应模式，即扩缩容控制器仅在检测到集群内需求后才调整资源，缺乏预测性措施，可能导致资源过度配置与成本上升，或资源配置不足引发性能下降。本文提出NimbusGuard——一个基于Kubernetes的开源自动扩缩容系统，其通过深度强化学习智能体实现主动式扩缩容。该系统采用长短期记忆模型预测未来工作负载模式，以增强智能体的感知能力。实验通过将NimbusGuard与内置扩缩容控制器（如水平Pod自动扩缩容器）及事件驱动扩缩容器KEDA进行对比评估，结果表明NimbusGuard的主动式框架在性能与成本效益方面均优于现有被动式方法。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of reactive autoscalers in Kubernetes, which can cause resource over-provisioning or under-provisioning, this paper introduces NimbusGuard, a proactive autoscaling framework. The method employs a deep reinforcement learning agent, specifically a Deep Q-Network, enhanced with a Long Short-Term Memory model to predict future workload patterns and preemptively adjust resources. Experimental comparisons against standard controllers like Horizontal Pod Autoscaler and KEDA show that NimbusGuard achieves better performance and cost efficiency by anticipating demand rather than reacting to it.
针对Kubernetes中反应式自动扩缩容机制易导致资源过度配置或不足的问题，本文提出了NimbusGuard这一主动式自动扩缩容框架。该方法采用深度强化学习智能体，结合长短期记忆模型预测未来工作负载模式，从而预先调整资源。通过与Horizontal Pod Autoscaler和KEDA等内置控制器的实验对比，结果表明NimbusGuard通过预测需求而非被动响应，在性能和成本效率方面均表现更优。
When Valid Signals Fail: Regime Boundaries Between LLM Features and RL Trading Policies
Authors: Zhengzhe Yang
First: 2026-04-13T04:53:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T04:53:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Can large language models (LLMs) generate continuous numerical features that improve reinforcement learning (RL) trading agents? We build a modular pipeline where a frozen LLM serves as a stateless feature extractor, transforming unstructured daily news and filings into a fixed-dimensional vector consumed by a downstream PPO agent. We introduce an automated prompt-optimization loop that treats the extraction prompt as a discrete hyperparameter and tunes it directly against the Information Coefficient - the Spearman rank correlation between predicted and realized returns - rather than NLP losses. The optimized prompt discovers genuinely predictive features (IC above 0.15 on held-out data). However, these valid intermediate representations do not automatically translate into downstream task performance: during a distribution shift caused by a macroeconomic shock, LLM-derived features add noise, and the augmented agent under-performs a price-only baseline. In a calmer test regime the agent recovers, yet macroeconomic state variables remain the most robust driver of policy improvement. Our findings highlight a gap between feature-level validity and policy-level robustness that parallels known challenges in transfer learning under distribution shift.
中文标题/摘要
标题：当有效信号失效时：大语言模型特征与强化学习交易策略间的机制边界
大语言模型能否生成可提升强化学习交易智能体性能的连续数值特征？我们构建了一个模块化流程：冻结的大语言模型作为无状态特征提取器，将非结构化的每日新闻与文件转化为固定维度的向量，供下游PPO智能体使用。我们引入了自动化提示优化循环，将提取提示视为离散超参数，并直接依据信息系数（预测收益与实际收益间的斯皮尔曼秩相关系数）而非自然语言处理损失进行调优。优化后的提示发现了真正具有预测性的特征（在保留数据上信息系数超过0.15）。然而，这些有效的中间表征并不能自动转化为下游任务性能：在宏观经济冲击引发的分布偏移期间，大语言模型衍生的特征会引入噪声，增强型智能体的表现逊于仅使用价格数据的基线。在更平稳的测试机制中智能体表现恢复，但宏观经济状态变量仍是策略改进最稳健的驱动因素。我们的研究揭示了特征层面有效性与策略层面鲁棒性之间的差距，这与分布偏移下迁移学习的已知挑战相呼应。
Summary / 总结
This study investigates whether large language models (LLMs) can generate continuous numerical features from unstructured financial text to enhance reinforcement learning (RL) trading agents. The method employs a modular pipeline where a frozen LLM acts as a stateless feature extractor, processing daily news and filings into fixed-dimensional vectors for a downstream PPO agent, and introduces an automated prompt-optimization loop that tunes the extraction prompt directly against the Information Coefficient (IC) metric. Experimental results show the optimized prompt yields predictive features with an IC above 0.15 on held-out data, but during a macroeconomic shock-induced distribution shift, these LLM-derived features add noise, causing the augmented agent to underperform a price-only baseline; in calmer regimes, the agent recovers, though macroeconomic state variables prove more robust for policy improvement, highlighting a gap between feature validity and policy robustness under distribution shift.
本研究探讨大型语言模型（LLM）能否从非结构化金融文本中生成连续数值特征以增强强化学习（RL）交易智能体。方法采用模块化流程，其中冻结的LLM作为无状态特征提取器，将每日新闻和文件处理为固定维度向量供下游PPO智能体使用，并引入自动化提示优化循环，直接针对信息系数（IC）指标调整提取提示。实验结果表明，优化后的提示在保留数据上产生了IC高于0.15的预测性特征，但在宏观经济冲击导致的分布偏移期间，这些LLM衍生特征增加了噪声，使得增强智能体表现不及仅使用价格数据的基线；在平稳测试环境中，智能体性能恢复，但宏观经济状态变量仍是策略改进最稳健的驱动因素，凸显了分布偏移下特征有效性与策略鲁棒性之间的差距。
Robust Adversarial Policy Optimization Under Dynamics Uncertainty
Authors: Mintae Kim, Koushil Sreenath
First: 2026-04-13T04:23:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T04:23:54+00:00
Comments: 33 pages, 8 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) policies often fail under dynamics that differ from training, a gap not fully addressed by domain randomization or existing adversarial RL methods. Distributionally robust RL provides a formal remedy but still relies on surrogate adversaries to approximate intractable primal problems, leaving blind spots that potentially cause instability and over-conservatism. We propose a dual formulation that directly exposes the robustness-performance trade-off. At the trajectory level, a temperature parameter from the dual problem is approximated with an adversarial network, yielding efficient and stable worst-case rollouts within a divergence bound. At the model level, we employ Boltzmann reweighting over dynamics ensembles, focusing on more adverse environments to the current policy rather than uniform sampling. The two components act independently and complement each other: trajectory-level steering ensures robust rollouts, while model-level sampling provides policy-sensitive coverage of adverse dynamics. The resulting framework, robust adversarial policy optimization (RAPO) outperforms robust RL baselines, improving resilience to uncertainty and generalization to out-of-distribution dynamics while maintaining dual tractability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：动态不确定性下的鲁棒对抗策略优化
强化学习策略常在训练环境之外的动态系统中失效，领域随机化或现有对抗性强化学习方法未能完全解决此问题。分布鲁棒强化学习提供了形式化解决方案，但仍依赖代理对抗器逼近难解的原问题，存在可能导致不稳定和过度保守的盲区。我们提出一种对偶形式，直接揭示鲁棒性与性能的权衡关系。在轨迹层面，通过对抗网络逼近对偶问题中的温度参数，在散度界内实现高效稳定的最坏情况推演。在模型层面，采用玻尔兹曼重加权方法处理动态系统集成，聚焦对当前策略更不利的环境而非均匀采样。两个组件独立运作且相互补充：轨迹层面引导确保鲁棒推演，模型层面采样提供对策略敏感的对抗动态覆盖。所提出的鲁棒对抗策略优化框架优于现有鲁棒强化学习基线，在保持对偶可解性的同时，提升了对不确定性的鲁棒性及对分布外动态的泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the vulnerability of reinforcement learning policies to dynamics shifts not fully mitigated by existing robust RL methods, which often rely on surrogate adversaries leading to instability or over-conservatism. The proposed method, robust adversarial policy optimization (RAPO), introduces a dual formulation to directly manage the robustness-performance trade-off: at the trajectory level, an adversarial network approximates a temperature parameter for efficient worst-case rollouts within a divergence bound, while at the model level, Boltzmann reweighting over dynamics ensembles prioritizes sampling more adverse environments to the current policy. Experimental results show that RAPO outperforms robust RL baselines, enhancing resilience to uncertainty and generalization to out-of-distribution dynamics while maintaining tractability.
本文针对强化学习策略在动态变化下的脆弱性问题，现有鲁棒强化学习方法常依赖代理对抗者，易导致不稳定或过度保守。提出的鲁棒对抗策略优化（RAPO）方法采用对偶公式直接处理鲁棒性与性能的权衡：在轨迹层面，通过对抗网络近似温度参数以在发散边界内生成高效的最坏情况推演；在模型层面，利用玻尔兹曼重加权对动态集成进行采样，优先关注对当前策略更不利的环境。实验结果表明，RAPO优于鲁棒强化学习基线，在保持可处理性的同时，提升了对不确定性的适应能力和对分布外动态的泛化性能。
MMR-AD: A Large-Scale Multimodal Dataset for Benchmarking General Anomaly Detection with Multimodal Large Language Models
Authors: Xincheng Yao, Zefeng Qian, Chao Shi, Jiayang Song, Chongyang Zhang
First: 2026-04-13T04:14:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T04:14:56+00:00
Comments: Accepted by CVPR2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In the progress of industrial anomaly detection, general anomaly detection (GAD) is an emerging trend and also the ultimate goal. Unlike the conventional single- and multi-class AD, general AD aims to train a general AD model that can directly detect anomalies in diverse novel classes without any retraining or fine-tuning on the target data. Recently, Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have shown great promise in achieving general anomaly detection due to their revolutionary visual understanding and language reasoning capabilities. However, MLLM's general AD ability remains underexplored due to: (1) MLLMs are pretrained on amounts of data sourced from the Web, these data still have significant gaps with the data in AD scenarios. Moreover, the image-text pairs during pretraining are also not specifically for AD tasks. (2) The current mainstream AD datasets are image-based and not yet suitable for post-training MLLMs. To facilitate MLLM-based general AD research, we present MMR-AD, which is a comprehensive benchmark for both training and evaluating MLLM-based AD models. With MMR-AD, we reveal that the AD performance of current SOTA generalist MLLMs still falls far behind the industrial requirements. Based on MMR-AD, we also propose a baseline model, Anomaly-R1, which is a reasoning-based AD model that learns from the CoT data in MMR-AD and is further enhanced by reinforcement learning. Extensive experiments show that our Anomaly-R1 achieves remarkable improvements over generalist MLLMs in both anomaly detection and localization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MMR-AD：基于多模态大语言模型的通用异常检测大规模多模态基准数据集
在工业异常检测的发展进程中，通用异常检测（GAD）作为新兴趋势和终极目标，与传统单类别/多类别异常检测不同，其旨在训练无需目标数据重训练或微调即可直接检测多类新异常的通用模型。近期，多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）凭借革命性的视觉理解与语言推理能力，在实现通用异常检测方面展现出巨大潜力。然而，MLLMs的通用异常检测能力仍待深入探索，原因在于：（1）MLLMs基于海量网络数据预训练，与异常检测场景数据存在显著差异，且预训练的图文对未针对异常检测任务优化；（2）当前主流异常检测数据集为图像格式，不适用于MLLMs的后训练。为推进基于MLLM的通用异常检测研究，本文提出综合性基准数据集MMR-AD，用于训练与评估MLLM异常检测模型。通过该数据集研究发现，当前先进通用MLLMs的异常检测性能仍远未达到工业需求。基于MMR-AD，我们进一步提出基线模型Anomaly-R1——一种基于推理的异常检测模型，通过MMR-AD中的思维链数据学习，并采用强化学习增强。大量实验表明，Anomaly-R1在异常检测与定位任务上均显著优于通用MLLMs。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces MMR-AD, a large-scale multimodal dataset designed to benchmark general anomaly detection (GAD) using multimodal large language models (MLLMs), motivated by the need to address the gap between MLLMs' web-based pretraining data and industrial anomaly detection scenarios, as current datasets are inadequate for post-training MLLMs. The method involves creating MMR-AD to train and evaluate MLLM-based AD models, and proposing a baseline model, Anomaly-R1, which leverages chain-of-thought reasoning data from MMR-AD and is enhanced with reinforcement learning. Experimental results show that current state-of-the-art generalist MLLMs underperform on industrial AD tasks, while Anomaly-R1 achieves significant improvements in both anomaly detection and localization compared to these MLLMs.
本文提出了MMR-AD，一个用于基于多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）的通用异常检测（GAD）基准的大规模多模态数据集，其动机在于解决MLLMs基于网络的预训练数据与工业异常检测场景之间的差距，因为现有数据集不适合MLLMs的后训练。方法包括构建MMR-AD以训练和评估基于MLLMs的异常检测模型，并提出一个基线模型Anomaly-R1，该模型利用MMR-AD中的思维链推理数据，并通过强化学习进行增强。实验结果表明，当前最先进的通用MLLMs在工业异常检测任务上表现不佳，而Anomaly-R1在异常检测和定位方面相比这些MLLMs取得了显著提升。
You Only Judge Once: Multi-response Reward Modeling in a Single Forward Pass
Authors: Yinuo Yang, Zixian Ma, Manasi Ganti, Jieyu Zhang, Ranjay Krishna
First: 2026-04-13T04:02:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T04:02:03+00:00
Comments: 9 pages, 4 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present a discriminative multimodal reward model that scores all candidate responses in a single forward pass. Conventional discriminative reward models evaluate each response independently, requiring multiple forward passes, one for each potential response. Our approach concatenates multiple responses with separator tokens and applies cross-entropy over their scalar scores, enabling direct comparative reasoning and efficient $N$-way preference learning. The multi-response design also yields up to $N\times$ wall-clock speedup and FLOPs reduction over conventional single-response scoring. To enable $N$-way reward evaluation beyond existing pairwise benchmarks, we construct two new benchmarks: (1) MR$^2$Bench-Image contains human-annotated rankings over responses from 8 diverse models; (2) MR$^2$Bench-Video is a large-scale video-based reward benchmark derived from 94K crowdsourced pairwise human judgments over video question-answering spanning 19 models, denoised via preference graph ensemble. Both benchmarks provide 4-response evaluation variants sampled from the full rankings. Built on a 4B vision-language backbone with LoRA fine-tuning and a lightweight MLP value head, our model achieves state-of-the-art results on six multimodal reward benchmarks, including MR$^2$Bench-Image, MR$^2$Bench-Video, and four other existing benchmarks. Our model outperforms existing larger generative and discriminative reward models. We further demonstrate that our reward model, when used in reinforcement learning with GRPO, produces improved policy models that maintain performance across standard multimodal benchmarks while substantially improving open-ended generation quality, outperforming a single-response discriminative reward model (RM) baseline by a large margin in both training stability and open-ended generation quality.
中文标题/摘要
标题：单次判定：单次前向传播中的多响应奖励建模
我们提出了一种判别式多模态奖励模型，可在单次前向传播中为所有候选响应评分。传统的判别式奖励模型需独立评估每个响应，需多次前向传播（每个潜在响应一次）。我们的方法通过分隔符将多个响应拼接，并在其标量分数上应用交叉熵，实现了直接比较推理和高效的N路偏好学习。多响应设计相比传统单响应评分，可获得高达N倍的实时加速和FLOPs降低。为超越现有成对基准实现N路奖励评估，我们构建了两个新基准：（1）MR²Bench-Image包含对8个不同模型响应的人工标注排序；（2）MR²Bench-Video是基于视频的大规模奖励基准，源自94K个众包视频问答人类成对判断（涵盖19个模型），通过偏好图集成去噪。两个基准均提供从完整排序中采样的4响应评估变体。基于4B视觉语言主干（采用LoRA微调和轻量MLP值头），我们的模型在六个多模态奖励基准（包括MR²Bench-Image、MR²Bench-Video和四个现有基准）上取得最先进成果，性能优于现有更大的生成式和判别式奖励模型。我们进一步证明，当该奖励模型与GRPO结合用于强化学习时，可产生改进的策略模型：在保持标准多模态基准性能的同时，显著提升开放式生成质量；在训练稳定性和开放式生成质量上均大幅超越单响应判别式奖励模型基线。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the inefficiency of conventional discriminative reward models that require multiple forward passes to score candidate responses independently, this paper introduces a multi-response reward model that evaluates all responses in a single forward pass. The method concatenates multiple responses with separator tokens and applies cross-entropy over their scalar scores, enabling direct comparative reasoning and efficient N-way preference learning, which yields up to N× speedup and FLOPs reduction. Experimental results show that the model, built on a 4B vision-language backbone with LoRA fine-tuning, achieves state-of-the-art performance on six multimodal benchmarks, including two newly constructed benchmarks (MR²Bench-Image and MR²Bench-Video), and when used in reinforcement learning, it improves policy models in training stability and open-ended generation quality.
本文针对传统判别式奖励模型需多次前向传播独立评分候选响应的低效问题，提出了一种多响应奖励模型，可在单次前向传播中评估所有响应。该方法通过分隔符连接多个响应并对其标量分数应用交叉熵，实现了直接比较推理和高效的N向偏好学习，从而带来高达N倍的加速和计算量减少。实验结果表明，该模型基于40亿参数视觉语言主干网络并结合LoRA微调，在六个多模态基准测试（包括新构建的MR²Bench-Image和MR²Bench-Video）中取得了最先进性能，且在强化学习中应用时，能提升策略模型的训练稳定性和开放式生成质量。
On the Use of Bi-Objective Evolutionary Algorithms for the Stochastic MKP under Dynamic Constraints
Authors: Ishara Hewa Pathiranage, Aneta Neumann
First: 2026-04-13T02:59:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T02:59:03+00:00
Comments: Accepted to publish in Genetic and Evolutionary Computation Conference (GECCO '26)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The multiple knapsack problem (MKP) generalizes the classical knapsack problem by assigning items to multiple knapsacks subject to capacity constraints. It is used to model many real-world resource allocation and scheduling problems. In practice, these optimization problems often involve stochastic and dynamic components. Evolutionary algorithms provide a flexible framework for addressing such problems under uncertainty and dynamic changes. In this paper, we investigate a stochastic and dynamic variant of MKP with chance constraints, where the item weights are modeled as independent normally distributed random variables and knapsack capacities change during the optimization process. We formulate the problem as a bi-objective optimization formulation that balances profit maximization and probabilistic capacity satisfaction at a given confidence level. We conduct an empirical comparison of four widely used multi-objective evolutionary algorithms (MOEAs), representing both decomposition- and dominance-based search paradigms. The algorithms are evaluated under varying uncertainty levels, confidence thresholds, and dynamic change settings. The results provide comparative insights into the behavior of decomposition-based and dominance-based MOEAs for stochastic MKP under dynamic constraints.
中文标题/摘要
标题：动态约束下随机多背包问题的双目标进化算法应用研究
多背包问题（MKP）通过将物品分配给多个受容量约束的背包，推广了经典背包问题，常用于建模现实世界的资源分配与调度问题。实践中这类优化问题常包含随机性与动态性。进化算法为处理不确定性和动态变化提供了灵活框架。本文研究具有机会约束的随机动态MKP变体，其中物品权重建模为独立正态分布随机变量，背包容量在优化过程中动态变化。我们将问题构建为双目标优化模型，在给定置信水平下平衡利润最大化与概率容量满足度。对四种广泛使用的多目标进化算法（MOEA）进行实证比较，涵盖基于分解和基于支配的搜索范式。算法在不同不确定性水平、置信阈值和动态变化场景下进行评估，结果为动态约束下随机MKP问题中两类MOEA的行为特性提供了对比性见解。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to address real-world resource allocation problems that involve uncertainty and dynamic changes, this paper investigates a stochastic and dynamic variant of the multiple knapsack problem (MKP) with chance constraints, where item weights are random variables and capacities change over time. The method formulates the problem as a bi-objective optimization balancing profit maximization and probabilistic capacity satisfaction, and empirically compares four multi-objective evolutionary algorithms (MOEAs) from decomposition- and dominance-based paradigms. Experimental results under varying uncertainty levels, confidence thresholds, and dynamic settings provide comparative insights into the behavior of these MOEAs for the stochastic MKP under dynamic constraints.
本文针对现实世界中涉及不确定性和动态变化的资源分配问题，研究了具有机会约束的随机动态多背包问题变体，其中物品权重为随机变量且背包容量随时间变化。方法将该问题表述为平衡利润最大化和概率容量满足的双目标优化，并实证比较了四种基于分解和支配的多目标进化算法。在不同不确定性水平、置信阈值和动态设置下的实验结果为这些算法在动态约束下的随机多背包问题中的行为提供了比较性见解。
Controlling Multimodal Conversational Agents with Coverage-Enhanced Latent Actions
Authors: Yongqi Li, Hao Lang, Tieyun Qian, Yongbin Li
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-01-12T13:13:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-13T02:40:35+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ACL 2026 (Main), camera-ready version
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Vision-language models are increasingly employed as multimodal conversational agents (MCAs) for diverse conversational tasks. Recently, reinforcement learning (RL) has been widely explored for adapting MCAs to various human-AI interaction scenarios. Despite showing great enhancement in generalization performance, fine-tuning MCAs via RL still faces challenges in handling the extremely large text token space. To address this, we learn a compact latent action space for RL fine-tuning instead. Specifically, we adopt the learning from observation mechanism to construct the codebook for the latent action space, where future observations are leveraged to estimate current latent actions that could further be used to reconstruct future observations. However, the scarcity of paired image-text data hinders learning a codebook with sufficient coverage. Thus, we leverage both paired image-text data and text-only data to construct the latent action space, using a cross-modal projector for transforming text embeddings into image-text embeddings. We initialize the cross-modal projector on paired image-text data, and further train it on massive text-only data with a novel cycle consistency loss to enhance its robustness. We show that our latent action based method outperforms competitive baselines on two conversation tasks across various RL algorithms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于覆盖增强隐式动作的多模态对话智能体控制
视觉语言模型正日益作为多模态对话智能体应用于多样化对话任务。近期，强化学习被广泛探索用于使多模态对话智能体适应不同的人机交互场景。尽管在泛化性能上展现出显著提升，但通过强化学习微调多模态对话智能体仍面临处理极大文本标记空间的挑战。为此，我们转而学习紧凑的隐式动作空间进行强化学习微调。具体而言，采用观察学习机制构建隐式动作空间的码本，利用未来观测估计当前隐式动作，进而重构未来观测。然而，配对图文数据的稀缺性阻碍了学习具有充分覆盖度的码本。因此，我们联合使用配对图文数据与纯文本数据构建隐式动作空间，通过跨模态投影器将文本嵌入转换为图文嵌入。该投影器在配对图文数据上初始化，并基于大规模纯文本数据通过新型循环一致性损失进一步训练以增强鲁棒性。实验表明，基于隐式动作的方法在两种对话任务上均优于多种强化学习算法的基线模型。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of fine-tuning multimodal conversational agents (MCAs) via reinforcement learning (RL), where the large text token space complicates optimization. The proposed method learns a compact latent action space for RL by constructing a codebook through a learning-from-observation mechanism, which estimates latent actions from future observations. To overcome the scarcity of paired image-text data for codebook coverage, the approach leverages both paired and text-only data, using a cross-modal projector initialized on paired data and further trained on text-only data with a cycle consistency loss. Experimental results demonstrate that this latent action-based method outperforms competitive baselines across two conversation tasks using various RL algorithms.
本文针对通过强化学习微调多模态对话代理时，因文本标记空间过大而导致的优化难题。所提方法通过学习一个紧凑的潜在动作空间来应对，该空间通过基于观察学习的机制构建码本，利用未来观测来估计当前潜在动作。为解决配对图像-文本数据稀缺导致的码本覆盖不足问题，该方法同时利用配对数据和纯文本数据，使用一个在配对数据上初始化、并通过循环一致性损失在大量纯文本数据上进一步训练以增强鲁棒性的跨模态投影器。实验结果表明，基于潜在动作的方法在两种对话任务上，使用多种强化学习算法均优于现有基线。
